[\[1a\]]
[\[1a.1\]{D3786}]@#/_/shes bar kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba bzhugs so/_/
[\[1b\]]
[\[1b.1\]]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_a b+hi sa ma ya a laM kA ra nA ma pradz+nyA pA ra mi to pa de sha shAs+t+ra kA ri kA/_bod skad du/_shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos
[\[1b.2\]]mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i tshig le'ur byas pa/_sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/_/nyan thos zhi ba tshol rnams kun shes nyid kyis
[\[1b.3\]]nyer zhir 'khrid mdzad gang yin dang /_/'gro la phan par byed rnams lam shes nyid kyis 'jig rten don sgrub mdzad pa gang /_/gang dang yang dag ldan pas thub rnams rnam pa kun ldan
[\[1b.4\]]sna tshogs 'di gsungs pa/_/nyan thos byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs bcas sangs rgyas kyi ni yum de la phyag 'tshal/_/rnam pa thams cad mkhyen nyid lam/_/ston pas 'di rnams
[\[1b.5\]]bshad pa gang /_/gzhan gyis myong ba ma yin te/_/chos spyod bcu yi bdag nyid kyi/_/mdo don dran pa la bzhag nas/_/blo dang ldan pas mthong 'gyur phyir/_/bde blag tu ni rtogs pa
[\[2a\]]
[\[2a.1\]]zhes/_/bya ba rtsam pa'i dgos pa yin/_/shes rab pha rol phyin pa ni/_/dngos po brgyad kyis yang dag bshad/_/rnam kun mkhyen nyid lam shes nyid/_/de nas thams cad shes pa nyid/_/rnam kun mngon
[\[2a.2\]]rdzogs rtogs pa dang /_/rtse mor phyin dang mthar gyis pa/_/skad cig gcig mngon rdzogs byang chub/_/chos kyi sku dang de rnam brgyad/_/sems bskyed pa dang gdams ngag dang /_/nges 'byed yan lag rnam bzhi dang /_/sgrub pa yi
[\[2a.3\]]ni rten gyur pa/_/chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin dang /_/dmigs pa dag dang ched dang ni/_/go cha 'jug pa'i bya ba dang /_/tshogs ni nges par 'byung bcas rnams/_/thub pa'i rnam kun mkhyen pa nyid/_/mog mog por byed la sogs
[\[2a.4\]]dang /_/slob ma bse ru'i lam gang dang /_/'di dang gzhan pa'i yon tan gyis/_/phan yon che ba mthong ba'i lam/_/byed pa dang ni mos pa dang /_/bstod dang bkur dang bsngags pa dang /_/bsngo dang rjes su yi rang ba/_/yid la byed
[\[2a.5\]]pa bla med dag_/sgrub dang shin tu dag pa zhes/_/bya ba 'di ni sgom pa'i lam/_/byang chub sems dpa' mkhas rnams kyi/_/lam shes nyid ni de 'drar bshad/_/shes pas srid la mi gnas shing /_/snying rjes zhi la mi gnas dang /_/_
[\[2b\]]
[\[2b.1\]]thabs ma yin pas ring ba dang /_/thabs kyis ring ba ma yin nyid/_/mi mthun gnyen po'i phyogs dag dang /_/sbyor dang de yi mnyam nyid dang /_/nyan thos la sogs mthong ba'i lam/_/de 'dra kun shes nyid du 'dod/_/rnam pa sbyor bar bcas rnams dang /_/yon tan skyon
[\[2b.2\]]ni mtshan nyid bcas/_/thar dang nges 'byed cha mthun dang /_/slob pa phyir mi ldog pa'i tshogs/_/srid dang zhi ba mnyam nyid dang /_/zhing dag bla na med pa ni/_/rnam kun mngon rdzogs rtogs pa ste/_/'di ni thabs mkhas bcas pa yin/_/de yi rtags dang rnam 'phel dang /_/_
[\[2b.3\]]brtan dang sems kun gnas pa dang /_/mthong zhes bya dang sgom pa zhes/_/bya ba'i lam ni so so la/_/rnam par rtog pa rnam bzhi yi/_/gnyen po rnam pa bzhi dang ni/_/bar chad med pa'i ting nge 'dzin/_/log par sgrub dang bcas pa ni/_/rtse mo'i mngon rtogs mthar gyis
[\[2b.4\]]pa/_/rnam gsum rnam bcu skad cig ma/_/gcig gis mngon rdzogs byang chub pa/_/mtshan nyid kyis ni rnam pa bzhi/_/ngo bo nyid longs rdzogs bcas dang /_/de bzhin gzhan pa sprul pa ni/_/chos sku mdzad pa dang bcas pa/_/rnam pa bzhir ni yang dag brjod/_/_
[\[2b.5\]]sems bskyed pa ni gzhan don phyir/_/yang dag rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'dod/_/de dang de ni mdo bzhin du/_/bsdus dang rgyas pa'i sgo nas brjod/_/de yang sa gser zla ba me/_/gter dang rin chen 'byung gnas mtsho/_/rdo rje ri sman bshes gnyen dang /_/yid
[\[2b.6\]]bzhin nor bu nyi ma glu/_/rgyal po mdzod dang lam po che/_/bzhon pa bkod ma'i chu dang ni/_/sgra brnyan chu bo sprin rnams kyis/_/rnam pa nyi shu rtsa gnyis so/_/sgrub dang bden pa rnams dang ni/_/sangs rgyas la sogs dkon mchog gsum/_/ma zhen yongs su mi ngal dang /_/_
[\[2b.7\]]lam ni yongs su 'dzin pa dang /_/spyan lnga dang ni mngon shes kyi/_/yon tan drug dang mthong lam dang /_/bsgom zhes bya la gdams ngag ni/_/bcu yi bdag nyid shes par bya/_/dbang po rtul dang rnon po dang /_/dad dang mthong thob rigs nas rigs/_/bar chad gcig par
[\[3a\]]
[\[3a.1\]]skyes nas dang /_/byed dang byed min 'og min 'gro/_/'phar gsum srid rtse'i mthar thug 'gro/_/gzugs kyi chags bcom mthong ba yi/_/chos la zhi lus mngon sum byed/_/bse ru dang ni nyi shu'o/_/dmigs pa dang ni rnam pa dang /_/sgyu dang yongs su
[\[3a.2\]]'dzin pa yis/_/byang chub sems dpa' skyob pa yi/_/drod sogs bdag nyid ji bzhin du/_/rnam rtog bzhi po ldan brten pa/_/chung dang 'bring dang chen po rnams/_/nyan thos bse ru lta bu dang /_/bcas pa dag las khyad par 'phags/_/dmigs pa mi rtag la sogs pa/_/_
[\[3a.3\]]bden pa'i rten can de yi ni/_/rnam pa mngon zhen la sogs 'gog_/theg pa gsum char 'thob pa'i rgyu/_/gzugs sogs 'du 'god gnas bral dang /_/gnas dang brtags dang brjod du med/_/gzugs sogs mi gnas de dag ni/_/de yi ngo bo rang bzhin med/_/de dag
[\[3a.4\]]gcig gi rang bzhin gcig_/de mi rtag sogs par mi gnas/_/de rnams de yi ngo bos stong /_/de dag gcig gi rang bzhin gcig_/chos rnams mi 'dzin gang yin dang /_/de dag mtshan mar mi mthong phyir/_/shes rab kyis ni yongs rtogs pa/_/thams cad dmigs su
[\[3a.5\]]med par ro/_/gzugs sogs ngo bo nyid med nyid/_/de med pa nyid ngo bo nyid/_/de dag skye med nges 'byung med/_/dag dang de dag mtshan ma med/_/de yi mtshan mar mi brten pas/_/mos min 'du shes med pa yin/_/ting 'dzin de yi byed pa nyid/_/lung ston pa dang
[\[3a.6\]]rlom pa zad/_/gsum po phan tshun ngo bo gcig_/ting 'dzin rnam par mi rtog pa/_/de ltar nges 'byed cha mthun ni/_/chung dang 'bring dang chen po yin/_/gzhi dang de yi gnyen po yis/_/gzung bar rtog pa rnam pa gnyis/_/rmongs dang phung sogs bye brag gis/_/de ni
[\[3a.7\]]so sor rnam pa dgu/_/rdzas dang brtags pa'i rten can gyis/_/'dzin pa'ang rnam pa gnyis su 'dod/_/rang dbang bdag sogs ngo bo dang /_/phung sogs rten las de bzhin no/_/sems mi 'gong ba nyid la sogs/_/ngo bo nyid med sogs ston byed/_/de yi mi mthun
[\[3b\]]
[\[3b.1\]]phyogs bor ba/_/rnam pa kun tu yongs 'dzin yin/_/rtogs pa yi ni chos drug dang /_/gnyen po dang ni spong ba dang /_/de dag yongs su gtugs pa dang /_/shes rab snying brtser bcas pa dang /_/slob ma thun mong min nyid dang /_/gzhan gyi don gyi go rims dang /_/_
[\[3b.2\]]ye shes rtsol ba mi mnga' bar/_/'jug pa'i rten la rigs shes bya/_/chos kyi dbyings la dbyer med phyir/_/rigs ni tha dad rung ma yin/_/rten pa'i chos kyi bye brag gis/_/de yi dbye ba yongs su brjod/_/dmigs pa chos rnams thams cad de/_/de yang dge la
[\[3b.3\]]sogs pa yin/_/'jig rten pa yi rtogs pa dang /_/gang dag 'jig rten 'das 'dod dang /_/zag bcas zag pa med chos dang /_/gang dag 'dus byas 'dus ma byas/_/slob mthun mong chos rnams dang /_/gang dag thub pa'i thun mong min/_/sems can kun
[\[3b.4\]]mchog nyid sems dang /_/spangs dang rtogs dang gsum po la/_/chen po gsum gyi rang byung gi_/ched du bya ba 'di shes bya/_/de dag so sor sbyin la sogs/_/rnam pa drug tu bsdus pa yis/_/go cha'i sgrub pa gang yin de/_/drug tshan drug gis ji bzhin
[\[3b.5\]]bshad/_/bsam gtan gzugs med sbyin sogs dang /_/lam dang byams la sogs pa dang /_/dmigs pa med dang ldan pa dang /_/'khor gsum rnam par dag pa dang /_/ched du bya dang mngon shes drug_/rnam kun mkhyen pa'i tshul la ni/_/'jug pa'i sgrub
[\[3b.6\]]pa theg chen la/_/'dzegs pa yin par shes par bya/_/brtse dang sbyin la sogs pa drug_/zhi gnas lhag mthong bcas pa dang /_/zung du 'brel ba'i lam gang dang /_/thabs la mkhas pa gang yin dang /_/ye shes dang ni bsod nams dang /_/lam dang gzungs
[\[3b.7\]]dang sa bcu dang /_/gnyen po tshogs kyi sgrub pa yi/_/rim pa yin par shes par bya/_/yongs su sbyong ba rnam bcu yis/_/sa ni dang po 'thob 'gyur te/_/bsam dang phan pa'i dngos nyid dang /_/sems can rnams la sems mnyam nyid/_/gtong dang bshes gnyen
[\[4a\]]
[\[4a.1\]]bsten pa dang /_/dam chos dmigs pa tshol ba dang /_/rtag tu nges 'byung sems nyid dang /_/sangs rgyas skur 'dod dga' ba dang /_/chos ston pa dang bden pa yi/_/tshig ni bcu pa yin par 'dod/_/'di dag rang bzhin mi dmigs pas/_/yongs su sbyong
[\[4a.2\]]bar shes par bya/_/tshul khrims byas pa gzo dang bzod/_/rab tu dga' dang snying brtse che/_/bkur sti bla ma la gus nyan/_/brgyad pa sbyin la sogs la brtson/_/thos pas mi ngoms nyid dang ni/_/zang zing med par chos sbyin dang /_/sangs rgyas zhing kun sbyong ba dang /_/_
[\[4a.3\]]'khor bas yongs su mi skyo dang /_/ngo tsha khrel yod ces bya ba/_/rlom med bdag nyid de rnam lnga/_/nags gnas 'dod chung chog shes dang /_/sbyangs pa yang dag sdom bsten dang /_/bslab pa yongs su mi gtong dang /_/'dod pa rnams la smod pa dang /_/mya ngan 'das
[\[4a.4\]]dang bdog kun gtong /_/mi zhum pa dang lta ba med/_/'dris dang khyim la 'khren pa dang /_/'du 'dzir gyur pa'i gnas dang ni/_/bdag bstod gzhan la brnyas pa dang /_/mi dge'i las kyi lam bcu dang /_/rlom pas khengs dang phyin ci log_/blo ngan dang ni nyon mongs
[\[4a.5\]]bzod/_/bcu po 'di ni rnam spangs na/_/sa lnga pa ni yang dag 'thob/_/sbyin dang tshul khrims bzod brtson 'grus/_/bsam gtan shes rab rab rdzogs pas/_/slob ma dang ni bse ru la/_/dga' dang skrag pa'i sems spangs pa/_/bslangs na mi zhum bdog pa kun/_/_
[\[4a.6\]]btang yang mi dga' med pa dang /_/dbul yang slong ba mi spong bas/_/sa ni drug pa yang dag 'thob/_/bdag dang sems can 'dzin pa dang /_/srog dang gang zag chad rtag dang /_/mtshan ma rgyu dang phung po dang /_/khams dang skye mched dag dang ni/_/khams gsum po la
[\[4a.7\]]gnas dang chags/_/sems ni kun tu zhum pa dang /_/dkon mchog gsum dang tshul khrims la/_/der lta ba yi mngon zhen dang /_/stong pa nyid la rtsod pa dang /_/de dang 'gal ba'i nyes pa ni/_/nyi shu gang la rnam chad pa/_/de yis sa ni bdun pa 'thob/_/rnam thar sgo
[\[4b\]]
[\[4b.1\]]gsum shes pa dang /_/'khor gsum rnam par dag nyid dang /_/snying rje dang ni rlom med dang /_/chos mnyam nyid dang tshul gcig shes/_/mi skye ba dang bzod shes dang /_/chos rnams rnam pa gcig tu ston/_/rtog pa kun tu 'joms pa dang /_/'du shes lta dang nyon mongs
[\[4b.2\]]spong /_/zhi gnas nges par sems pa dang /_/lhag mthong la ni mkhas pa dang /_/sems dul ba dang thams cad la/_/thogs pa med pa'i ye shes dang /_/chags pa'i sa min gar 'dod par/_/zhing gzhan du ni mnyam 'gro dang /_/kun tu bdag gi ngo bo ni/_/ston pa nyid
[\[4b.3\]]dang nyi shu'o/_/sems can kun yid shes pa dang /_/mngon par shes pas brtse ba dang /_/sangs rgyas zhing bzang sgrub pa dang /_/yongs su brtag phyir sangs rgyas brten/_/dbang po shes dang rgyal ba yi/_/zhing sbyong sgyu ma ltar gnas dang /_/bsams bzhin srid pa
[\[4b.4\]]len pa dang /_/las ni rnam pa 'di brgyad bshad/_/smon lam dag ni mtha' yas dang /_/lha la sogs pa'i skad shes dang /_/spobs pa chu bo lta bu dang /_/mngal du 'jug pa mchog dang ni/_/rigs dang rus dang cho 'brang dang /_/'khor dang skye ba dag dang ni/_/nges
[\[4b.5\]]'byung byang chub shing rnams dang /_/yon tan phun sum tshogs pa yin/_/sa dgu 'das nas ye shes ni/_/gang gis sangs rgyas sar gnas pa/_/de ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa/_/bcu pa yin par shes par bya/_/mthong dang sgom pa'i lam dag la/_/gzung
[\[4b.6\]]dang 'dzin pa'i rnam rtog rnams/_/nye bar zhi bar bya ba'i phyir/_/gnyen po rnam pa brgyad ces bya/_/ched du bya dang mnyam nyid dang /_/sems can don dang 'bad med dang /_/mtha' las 'das par nges 'byung dang /_/thob pa'i mtshan nyid nges 'byung dang /_/rnam pa
[\[4b.7\]]thams cad mkhyen nyid dang /_/lam gyi yul can nges 'byung ste/_/rnam pa brgyad kyi bdag nyid 'di/_/nges 'byung sgrub pa yin zhes bya/_/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/_skabs dang
[\[5a\]]
[\[5a.1\]]po'o//_//lha rnams rung bar bya ba'i phyir/_/'od kyis mog mog por mdzad dang /_/yul nges pa dang khyab pa dang /_/rang bzhin dang ni de yi las/_/lam shes nyid kyi tshul la ni/_/'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi dag gi/_/rnam pa mi
[\[5a.2\]]dmigs sgo nas ni/_/nyan thos lam 'di shes par bya/_/'phags pa nyan thos lam la ni/_/gzugs la sogs pa stong pa'i phyir/_/stong pa nyid rnams dbyer med pas/_/dro ba de dag mi dmigs pas/_/rtse mor gyur pa dag tu 'dod/_/de la rtag la sogs tshul
[\[5a.3\]]gyis/_/gnas pa bkag pas bzod pa rnams/_/sa bcu dag las brtsams nas ni/_/mi gnas rgyas par bstan pa yis/_/chos kyi mchog tu 'gyur bshad de/_/ci phyir zhe na sangs rgyas kyis/_/mkhyen nas chos rnams ma gzigs phyir/_/rang byung bdag nyid rtogs
[\[5a.4\]]pa'i phyir/_/gzhan gyis bstan yang mi dgos la/_/bse ru lta bu'i ye shes ni/_/zab pa nyid du mngon par brjod/_/gang gang don ni gang gang la/_/ji lta ji ltar nyan 'dod pa/_/de de la don de dang de/_/sgra med kyang de de ltar snang /_/gzung don rtog pa spong phyir dang /_/_
[\[5a.5\]]'dzin pa mi spong phyir dang ni/_/rten gyis bse ru lta bu'i lam/_/yang dag bsdus par shes par bya/_/btags pa'i chos nyid mi 'gal bar/_/ston pa'i rnam pa dror gyur pa/_/rtse mor gyur pa gzugs la sogs/_/'grib pa med la sogs pas phye/_/nang stong nyid
[\[5a.6\]]la sogs pa yis/_/gzugs sogs mi 'dzin phyir bzod pa/_/gzugs sogs skye ba med sogs kyi/_/rnam pa can ni chos kyi mchog_/bden dang bden la bzod pa dang /_/shes pa'i skad cig rnam bzhi yis/_/lam shes nyid la mthong ba'i lam/_/phan yon bcas
[\[5a.7\]]pa 'di bshad do/_/de bzhin nyid dang sangs rgyas dag_/phan tshun rten pa rten med phyir/_/rnam grangs khas mi len pa dang /_/chen po tshad ma med bcas dang /_/tshad med pa dang mtha' med dang /_/der gnas gzugs la sogs pa la/_/sangs rgyas nyid du nges 'dzin dang /_/_
[\[5b\]]
[\[5b.1\]]blang med dor ba med sogs dang /_/byams la sogs pa stong nyid dang /_/sangs rgyas nyid ni 'thob pa dang /_/rnam par byang kun yongs bsdus dang /_/nyam nga ba dang nad kun sel/_/mya ngan 'das 'dzin zhi nyid dang /_/sangs rgyas rnams kyis bsrung la sogs/_/srog mi
[\[5b.2\]]gcod pa la sogs pa/_/rnam pa kun mkhyen tshul la ni/_/bdag nyid gnas te sems can dag_/'god dang sbyin pa la sogs pa/_/rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu bsngo ba/_/lam shes nyid kyi skad cig ma/_/kun nas zhi dang thams cad la/_/bdud dang nyon mongs las rgyal
[\[5b.3\]]dang /_/gnod pas brdzi ba med nyid dang /_/byang chub dang ni rten mchod nyid/_/mos pa rang gi don dang ni/_/rang gzhan don dang gzhan don dang /_/rnam gsum shes bya de yang ni/_/chung dang 'bring dang chen po ste/_/so sor rnam pa gsum du 'dod/_/chung ngu'i chung sogs dbye ba yis/_/de
[\[5b.4\]]yang rnam gsum de ltar na/_/rnam pa nyi shu bdun du 'dod/_/shes rab pha rol phyin pa la/_/mos pa'i gnas skabs rnams la ni/_/dgu tshan gsum gyis bstod pa dang /_/bkur ba dang ni bsngags par 'dod/_/yongs su bsngo ba khyad par can/_/de yi byed pa mchog
[\[5b.5\]]yin no/_/de ni dmigs med rnam pa can/_/phyin ci ma log mtshan nyid do/_/dben dang sangs rgyas bsod nams tshogs/_/rang bzhin dran pa'i spyod yul can/_/thabs bcas mtshan ma med pa dang /_/sangs rgyas rjes su yi rang dang /_/khams gsum rtogs pa ma yin
[\[5b.6\]]dang /_/chung dang 'bring dang chen po yi/_/bsngo ba gzhan ni rnam gsum po/_/bsod nams che 'byung bdag nyid do/_/thabs dang mi dmigs pa dag gis/_/dge ba'i rtsa la yi rang ba/_/rjes su yi rang yid byed pa/_/bsgom pa yin par 'dir brjod do/_/de yi ngo bo nyid
[\[5b.7\]]mchog nyid/_/kun la mngon par 'du mi byed/_/chos rnams dmigs su med par ni/_/gtod par byed pa don chen nyid/_/sangs rgyas bsten dang sbyin sogs dang /_/thabs la mkhas pa gang yin pa/_/'di la mos pa'i rgyu dag yin/_/chos kyis phongs pa'i rgyu
[\[6a\]]
[\[6a.1\]]dag ni/_/bdud kyi thibs kyis non pa dang /_/zab mo'i chos la ma mos dang /_/phung po la sogs mngon zhen dang /_/sdig pa'i grogs pos yongs zin pa'o/_/'bras bu dag pa gzugs la sogs/_/dag pa nyid de gang gi phyir/_/de gnyis tha
[\[6a.2\]]dad ma yin zhing /_/bcad du med pas dag par brjod/_/nyon mongs shes bya lam gsum gyi/_/nyams phyir slob ma bse ru dang /_/rgyal sras rnams kyi dag pa ste/_/sangs rgyas rnam kun shin tu ba/_/sa dgu la ni chen po yi/_/chen po la sogs dri ma yi/_/gnyen po
[\[6a.3\]]chung ngu'i chung ngu la/_/sogs pa'i lam ni dag pa yin/_/de la klan ka spangs pa yis/_/lam ni 'jal dang gzhal bya dag_/mnyam pa nyid kyis khams gsum gyi/_/gnyen po nyid du 'dod pa yin/_/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par
[\[6a.4\]]rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/_skabs gnyis pa'o//_//tshu rol pha rol mtha' la min/_/de dag bar na mi gnas pa/_/dus rnams mnyam pa nyid shes phyir/_/shes rab pha rol phyin par 'dod/_/de ni mtshan mar dmigs sgo nas/_/thabs
[\[6a.5\]]ma yin pas ring ba ste/_/de ni thabs la mkhas pa yis/_/yang dag nye ba nyid du bshad/_/gzugs sogs phung po stong nyid dang /_/dus gsum rtogs pa'i chos rnams dang /_/sbyin sogs byang chub phyogs rnams la/_/spyod pa'i 'du shes mi mthun phyogs/_/sbyin la
[\[6a.6\]]sogs la ngar 'dzin med/_/gzhan dag de la 'dzud byed pa/_/de ni chags pa'i mtha' 'gog pas/_/rgyal la sogs la chags pa phra/_/chos kyi lam ni rang bzhin gyis/_/dben pa'i phyir na de zab nyid/_/chos rnams rang bzhin gcig par ni/_/shes pas chags pa spong ba yin/_/_
[\[6a.7\]]mthong ba la sogs bkag pa yis/_/de ni rtogs par dka' bar bshad/_/gzugs la sogs par mi shes phyir/_/de ni bsam mi khyab par 'dod/_/de ltar kun shes nyid lugs la/_/mi mthun gnyen po'i phyogs dag gi_/rnam par dbye ba ma lus pa/_/ji skad bshad pa 'dir
[\[6b\]]
[\[6b.1\]]shes bya/_/gzugs sogs de mi rtag sogs dang /_/de ma rdzogs dang rab rdzogs dang /_/de la chags pa med nyid la/_/spyod pa bkag pa'i sbyor ba dang /_/mi 'gyur byed po med nyid dang /_/bya dka' rnam gsum sbyor ba dang /_/skal ba ji bzhin 'bras thob pas/_/'bras yod
[\[6b.2\]]'dod pa de dang ni/_/gzhan la rag las med gang dang /_/snang ba rnam bdun shes byed do/_/gzugs la sogs la rlom med pa/_/rnam bzhi de yi mnyam pa nyid/_/sdug bsngal la sogs bden pa la/_/chos shes rjes su shes pa dang /_/bzod shes skad cig bdag nyid 'di/_/_
[\[6b.3\]]kun shes tshul la mthong ba'i lam/_/gzugs rtag ma yin mi rtag min/_/mtha' las 'das dang rnam dag dang /_/ma skyes ma 'gags la sogs dang /_/mkha' 'dra chags pa spangs pa dang /_/yongs su 'dzin las grol ba dang /_/ngo bo nyid kyis brjod med dang /_/_
[\[6b.4\]]gang phyir 'di don brjod pa yis/_/gzhan la sbyin du med pa dang /_/dmigs pa med par byed pa dang /_/shin tu rnam dag nad mi 'byung /_/ngan song chad dang 'bras bu ni/_/mngon du bya la mi rtog nyid/_/mtshan ma dag dang ma 'brel dang /_/dngos dang ming dang gnyis po
[\[6b.5\]]la/_/shes pa skye ba med pa ni/_/kun shes nyid kyi skad cig ma/_/de ltar 'di dang yang 'di dang /_/yang 'di yin te rnam gsum po/_/'di ni gnas skabs gsum po dag_/rdzogs par yongs su bstan pa yin/_/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan
[\[6b.6\]]bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/_skabs gsum pa'o//_//gzhi shes pa yi bye brag rnams/_/rnam pa zhes bya mtshan nyid de/_/kun mkhyen nyid ni rnam gsum phyir/_/de ni rnam pa gsum du 'dod/_/med pa'i rnam pa
[\[6b.7\]]nas bzung ste/_/mi g.yo ba yi rnam pa'i bar/_/bden pa so so la bzhi dang /_/lam la de ni bco lngar bshad/_/rgyu dang lam dang sdug bsngal dang /_/'gog pa la ni go rims bzhin/_/de dag brgyad dang bdun dang ni/_/lnga dang bcu drug ces bsgrags so/_/_
[\[7a\]]
[\[7a.1\]]dran pa nyer gzhag nas bzung ste/_/sangs rgyas rnam pa'i mthar thug rnams/_/lam gyi bden pa'i rjes mthun par/_/kun mkhyen gsum du phye bas na/_/slob ma byang chub sems dpa' dang /_/sangs rgyas rnams la rim bzhin du/_/sum cu
[\[7a.2\]]bdun dang sum cu bzhi/_/sum cu rtsa dgu dag tu bzhed/_/sangs rgyas rnams la lhag par byas/_/de la dge ba'i rtsa ba bskrun/_/dge ba'i bshes kyi mgon bcas pa/_/'di mnyan pa yi snod yin no/_/sangs rgyas bstan dang kun 'dri dang /_/sbyin dang tshul
[\[7a.3\]]khrims sogs spyod pas/_/len dang 'dzin la sogs pa yi/_/snod du dam pa rnams bzhed do/_/gzugs la sogs la mi gnas phyir/_/de la sbyor ba bkag pa'i phyir/_/de yi de bzhin nyid zab phyir/_/de rnams gting dpag dka' ba'i phyir/_/de dag tshad ni
[\[7a.4\]]med phyir dang /_/tshegs chen yun ring rtogs pa'i phyir/_/lung bstan phyir mi ldog nyid dang /_/nges 'byung bar chad med bcas dang /_/byang chub nye dang myur ba dang /_/gzhan don 'phel med 'grib med phyir/_/chos dang chos min sogs mi mthong /_/gzugs
[\[7a.5\]]sogs bsam mi khyab mi mthong /_/gzugs sogs de yi mtshan ma dang /_/de yi ngo bor rnam mi rtog_/'bras bu rin chen sbyin byed dang /_/de ni dag pa mtshams dang bcas/_/bdud kyi mthu bcom la sogs pa/_/yon tan rnam pa bcu bzhi'o/_/skyon ni bcu
[\[7a.6\]]tshan bzhir bcas pa/_/drug tu nges par rtogs par bya/_/gang gi mtshon te mtshan nyid du/_/shes bya de yang rnam pa gsum/_/shes pa khyad par byed pa ste/_/ngo bo nyid gang mtshon bya yang /_/de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba dang /_/'jig rten 'jig med bdag
[\[7a.7\]]nyid dang /_/sems can sems kyi spyod pa dang /_/de bsdus pa dang phyir ltas dang /_/mi bzad pa yi rnam pa dang /_/chags bcas sogs dang rgya chen dang /_/chen por gyur dang tshad med dang /_/rnam shes bstan du med pa dang /_/sems bltar med dang shes pa de/_/_
[\[7b\]]
[\[7b.1\]]g.yo ba la sogs shes bya dang /_/de las gzhan yang de dag ni/_/de bzhin nyid kyi rnam par shes/_/thub pas de bzhin nyid rtogs te/_/gzhan la bstan pa zhes bya 'di/_/thams cad shes pa nyid skabs kyi/_/shes pa'i mtshan nyid bsdus pa yin/_/stong nyid mtshan med
[\[7b.2\]]bcas pa dang /_/smon pa rnam par spangs pa dang /_/skye med 'gag pa med sogs dang /_/chos nyid rnam par 'khrug med dang /_/'du mi byed dang rnam mi rtog_/rab dbye mtshan nyid med nyid la/_/lam shes nyid kyi skabs kyis ni/_/shes pa'i mtshan nyid yin par bzhed/_/_
[\[7b.3\]]de ni nyid kyi chos bsten nas/_/gnas dang gus par bya ba dang /_/bla ma nyid dang mnyes pa dang /_/de la mchod dang byed med dang /_/kun tu 'jug mkhyen gang yin dang /_/ma mthong ston par mdzad pa dang /_/'jig rten stong nyid rnam pa dang /_/brjod dang shes mdzad mngon sum
[\[7b.4\]]mdzad/_/bsam mi khyab dang zhi nyid ston/_/'jig rten 'du shes 'gog pa la/_/rnam pa kun mkhyen tshul la ni/_/shes pa'i mtshan nyid ces bshad do/_/bsam mi khyab sogs khyad par gyis/_/khyad zhugs bden pa'i spyod yul can/_/skad cig ma ni bcu drug
[\[7b.5\]]gis/_/khyad par mtshan nyid bshad pa yin/_/bsam mi khyab dang mi mnyam dang /_/gzhal dang bgrang las yang dag 'das/_/'phags pa kun bsdus mkhas pa yis/_/rig bya thun mong min shes nyid/_/shes myur bri dang gang med dang /_/sgrub dang yang dag
[\[7b.6\]]'grub pa dang /_/dmigs pa brtan dang bcas pa dang /_/mtha' dag pa dang yongs 'dzin dang /_/ro myang med dang khyad par ni/_/bcu drug bdag nyid ces bya ste/_/gang gis lam ni gzhan dag las/_/khyad du 'phags pas khyad par lam/_/phan dang bde dang skyob pa
[\[7b.7\]]dang /_/mi rnams kyi ni skyabs dag dang /_/gnas dang dpung gnyen gling dang ni/_/yongs 'dren pa zhes bya ba dang /_/lhun gyis grub dang theg gsum gyis/_/'bras bu mngon sum mi byed dag_/tha ma rten gyi mdzad pa ste/_/'di ni byed pa'i mtshan nyid yin/_/nyon
[\[8a\]]
[\[8a.1\]]mongs rtags dang mtshan ma dang /_/mi mthun phyogs dang gnyen po dag_/dben dang dka' dang nges pa dang /_/ched du bya dang mi dmigs dang /_/mngon par zhen pa bkag pa dang /_/dmigs pa zhes bya gang yin dang /_/mi mthun thogs pa med dang de/_/_
[\[8a.2\]]gzhi med 'gro med skye med dang /_/de bzhin nyid ni mi dmigs dang /_/ngo bo nyid bcu drug bdag nyid/_/mtshon bya lta bur mtshon pas na/_/mtshan nyid bzhi par bzhed pa yin/_/mtshan med rab tu sbyin la sogs/_/yang dag sgrub la mkhas pa ni/_/rnam pa thams cad
[\[8a.3\]]rtogs 'di la/_/thar pa'i cha dang mthun par 'dod/_/sangs rgyas sogs dmigs dad pa dang /_/sbyin sogs spyod yul brtson 'grus dang /_/bsam pa phun tshogs dran pa dang /_/rnam par mi rtog ting 'dzin dang /_/chos rnams rnam pa thams cad du/_/shes pa'i shes
[\[8a.4\]]rab dang rnam lnga/_/rdzogs pa'i byang chub rnon po yis/_/rtogs sla rtul pos rtogs dkar bzhed/_/dro ba rnams kyi dmigs pa 'dir/_/sems can thams cad yin par bsngags/_/de dag nyid la sems mnyam sogs/_/rnam pa dag ni bcur bshad do/_/bdag nyid sdig
[\[8a.5\]]pa las ldog cing /_/sbyin la sogs la gnas pas gzhan/_/de dag la ni 'god pa dang /_/bsngags pa brjod dang mthun pa nyid/_/rtser gyur de bzhin bzod pa ni/_/rang gzhan rten can bden shes pa/_/chos mchog de bzhin sems can rnams/_/smin byed sogs
[\[8a.6\]]kyis shes par bya/_/nges 'byed yan lag nas bzung ste/_/mthong dang sgom pa'i lam dag la/_/byang chub sems dpa' gang dag gnas/_/de 'dir mi ldog pa yi tshogs/_/gzugs la sogs las ldog sogs rtags/_/rnam pa nyi shur brjod pa yis/_/nges
[\[8a.7\]]'byed yan lag la gnas pa'i/_/phyir mi ldog pa'i mtshan nyid 'di/_/gzugs la sogs las ldog pa dang /_/the tshom mi ngal zad pa dang /_/bdag nyid dge ba la gnas shing /_/gzhan dag de la 'god pa dang /_/gzhan gyi rten can sbyin sogs dang /_/zab mo'i
[\[8b\]]
[\[8b.1\]]don la'ang som nyi med/_/byams lus sogs dang sgrib pa ni/_/rnam pa lnga dang mi 'grogs dang /_/bag la nyal kun 'joms pa dang /_/dran pa dang ni shes bzhin dang /_/gos la sogs pa gtsang ba dang /_/lus la srin bu rnams mi 'byung /_/gya gyu med
[\[8b.2\]]sems sbyangs pa ni/_/len dang ser sna med sogs dang /_/chos nyid ldan par 'gro nyid dang /_/sems can don du dmyal tshol dang /_/gzhan gyis bkri bar mi btub dang /_/lam gzhan nye bar ston bdud la/_/bdud ces bya bar rtogs pa dang /_/sangs rgyas
[\[8b.3\]]dgyes pa'i spyod pa ste/_/rtags ni nyi shu de dag gis/_/drod dang rtse mo bzod bcas dang /_/chos mchog rnams la gnas pa ni/_/rdzogs pa'i byang chub las mi ldog_/mthong ba'i lam la bzod pa dang /_/shes pa'i skad cig bcu drug ni/_/byang chub sems dpa' mi
[\[8b.4\]]ldog pa'i/_/mtshan nyid yin par shes par bya/_/gzugs sogs 'du shes ldog pa dang /_/sems brten theg pa dman dag las/_/rnam log bsam gtan la sogs pa'i/_/yan lag yongs su zad pa dang /_/lus sems yang ba nyid dang ni/_/'dod la spyod la
[\[8b.5\]]thabs mkhas dang /_/rtag tu tshangs par spyod nyid dang /_/'tsho ba rnam par dag nyid dang /_/phung sogs bar chad byed rnams dang /_/tshogs dang dbang sogs bcas pa yi/_/g.yul 'gyed ser sna la sogs la/_/sbyor dang rjes su sbyor ba yi/_/gnas pa so sor
[\[8b.6\]]bkag pa dang /_/chos ni rdul tsam mi dmigs nyid/_/rang gi sa la nges pa nyid/_/sa gsum la ni gnas pa dang /_/chos kyi don du srog gtong ba/_/de 'dra'i skad cig bcu drug ni/_/blo ldan mthong ba'i lam gnas pa'i/_/phyir mi ldog pa'i rtags dag yin/_/_
[\[8b.7\]]sgom pa'i lam ni zab pa ste/_/zab mo stong pa nyid la sogs/_/zab pa de ni sgro 'dogs dang /_/skur pa'i mtha' las grol ba nyid/_/nges 'byed yan lag dang mthong ba'i/_/lam dang sgom pa'i lam nyid la/_/yang dang yang du sems pa dang /_/'jal dang
[\[9a\]]
[\[9a.1\]]nges rtog sgom pa'i lam/_/de ni rgyun chags yin pa'i phyir/_/chung dang 'bring dang chen po rnams/_/chung ngu'i chung sogs dbye ba yis/_/rnam pas rnam pa dgur bzhed do/_/grangs med la sogs bstan pa rnams/_/dam pa'i don du bzod ma yin/_/_
[\[9a.2\]]kun rdzob tu ni thugs brtse bas/_/rgyu mthun de dag thub pa bzhed/_/dngos po brjod du med pa la/_/nyams pa dang ni 'phel mi rung /_/sgom zhes bya ba'i lam gyis ni/_/ci zhig nyams shing ci zhig 'thob/_/byang chub ji lta de bzhin du/_/'di ni 'dod pa'i don sgrub
[\[9a.3\]]byed/_/byang chub de bzhin nyid mtshan nyid/_/de yang de yi mtshan nyid bzhed/_/sems ni snga mas byang chub par/_/rigs min phyi mas kyang ni min/_/mar me'i dpe yi tshul gyis ni/_/zab mo'i chos nyid rnam pa brgyad/_/skye ba dang ni 'gag pa dang /_/de bzhin
[\[9a.4\]]nyid dang shes bya dang /_/shes dang spyod dang gnyis med dang /_/thabs mkhas pa la zab pa nyid/_/chos rnams rmi lam 'dra ba'i phyir/_/srid dang zhi bar mi rtog pa/_/las med la sogs klan ka yi/_/lan ni ji skad bshad par zad/_/sems can 'jig rten de
[\[9a.5\]]bzhin du/_/snod kyi 'jig rten ma dag pa/_/de la dag par sgrub pa yis/_/sangs rgyas zhing ni dag pa nyid/_/yul dang sbyor ba can 'di ni/_/dgra rnams las ni 'das pa dang /_/mi shes ji bzhin shugs dang ni/_/thun mong ma yin mtshan nyid dang /_/ma chags
[\[9a.6\]]pa dang mi dmigs dang /_/mtshan ma smon lam zad pa dang /_/de yi rtags dang tshad med pa/_/thabs la mkhas pa rnam pa bcu/_/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/_skabs bzhi pa'o//_//_
[\[9a.7\]]rmi lam na yang chos rnams kun/_/rmi lam lta bur lta la sogs/_/rtse mor phyin par sbyor ba'i rtags/_/rnam pa bcu gnyis dag tu bzhed/_/'dzam bu'i gling gi skye bo rnyed/_/sangs rgyas mchod pa'i dge la sogs/_/rnam mang du ni dper mdzad nas/_/rnam 'phel bcu
[\[9b\]]
[\[9b.1\]]drug bdag nyid do/_/kun mkhyen nyid gsum chos rnams kyi/_/yongs su rdzogs pa bla med pa/_/sems can don yongs mi gtong ba/_/bstan pa zhes ni mngon par brjod/_/gling bzhi pa dang stong dag dang /_/stong gnyis gsum dag dper mdzad nas/_/bsod nams
[\[9b.2\]]mang po nyid kyis ni/_/ting 'dzin yongs su bsgrags pa yin/_/'jug pa dang ni ldog pa la/_/gzung ba'i rnam rtog so sor de/_/dgu yi bdag nyid ji bzhin yul/_/min pa'i bdag nyid dag shes bya/_/so so'i skye bo 'phags dbye bas/_/sems can rdzas dang btags
[\[9b.3\]]yod par/_/rnam rtog 'dzin pa dag tu 'dod/_/de dag so sor dgu bdag nyid/_/gal te gzung don de bzhin med/_/de dag gang gi 'dzin par 'dod/_/de ltar de dag 'dzin pa yi/_/ngo bos stong pa'i mtshan nyid do/_/ngo bo nyid dang rigs dang ni/_/lam ni yang dag 'grub
[\[9b.4\]]pa dang /_/shes pa'i dmigs pa ma 'khrul dang /_/mi mthun phyogs dang gnyen po dang /_/rang gis rtogs dang byed pa dang /_/de yi las bya'i 'bras bu la/_/'jug pa'i phyogs kyi rten can gyi/_/rnam rtog de ni rnam dgur 'dod/_/srid dang zhi bar ltung ba'i phyir/_/_
[\[9b.5\]]rtogs pa dman pa nyid dang ni/_/yongs su 'dzin pa med pa dang /_/lam gyi rnam pa ma tshang dang /_/gzhan gyi rkyen gyis 'gro ba dang /_/ched du bya ba log pa dang /_/nyi tshe ba dang sna tshogs nyid/_/gnas dang 'jug la rmongs pa dang /_/rjes la 'gro zhes bya ba la/_/_
[\[9b.6\]]rnam rtog dgu yi bdag nyid 'di/_/ldog pa'i phyogs kyi rten can te/_/nyan thos la sogs yid la 'byung /_/'dzin pa dang ni 'dor ba dang /_/yid la byed dang khams rnams ni/_/gsum po dag dang nye 'brel dang /_/gnas dang mngon par zhen pa dang /_/chos kyi
[\[9b.7\]]dngos po brtags pa dang /_/chags pa dang ni gnyen po dang /_/ji ltar 'dod bzhin 'gro nyams la/_/'dzin pa dang por shes par bya/_/ched bzhin nges par mi 'byung dang /_/lam la lam min nges 'dzin dang /_/'gag dang bcas pa'i skye ba dang /_/dngos
[\[10a\]]
[\[10a.1\]]po ldan dang mi ldan dang /_/gnas dang rigs ni 'dzin pa dang /_/don du gnyer dang rgyu med dang /_/phyir rgal ba ni dmigs pa la/_/'dzin pa'i rnam rtog gzhan yin no/_/byang chub la gzhan ston pa dang /_/de yi rgyu ni yongs gtod dang /_/de
[\[10a.2\]]thob bar chad med pa'i rgyu/_/bsod nams mang po'i mtshan nyid do/_/dri ma zad dang mi skye ba'i/_/ye shes byang chub ces brjod do/_/zad med skye med phyir de dag_/go rims bzhin du shes par bya/_/'gog pa med pa'i rang bzhin la/_/mthong zhes bya ba'i lam gyis ni/_/_
[\[10a.3\]]rnam par rtog rigs ci zhig zad/_/skye med rnam pa ci zhig 'thob/_/gzhan gyis chos rnams kyang yod la/_/shes bya la yang ston pa yi/_/sgrib pa zad par brjod pa gang /_/de la kho bos mtshar du brtsis/_/'di las bsal bya ci yang med/_/gzhag par bya ba
[\[10a.4\]]cung zad med/_/yang dag nyid la yang dag lta/_/yang dag mthong na rnam par grol/_/sbyin pa la sogs re rer ni/_/de dag phan tshun bsdus pa gang /_/skad cig gcig pa'i bzod pa yis/_/bsdus pa de 'dir mthong ba'i lam/_/de nas seng ge rnam bsgyings pa'i/_/_
[\[10a.5\]]ting nge 'dzin la snyoms zhugs nas/_/rten cing 'brel 'byung lugs mthun dang /_/lugs mi mthun la rtog par byed/_/'gog dang bcas pa'i snyoms 'jug dgur/_/rnam pa gnyis su song 'ongs nas/_/'dod par gtogs pa'i rnam par shes/_/mnyam gzhag
[\[10a.6\]]min pa'i mtshams bzung ste/_/thod rgal du ni snyoms 'jug pa/_/gcig dang gnyis gsum bzhi dang lnga/_/drug dang bdun dang brgyad rgal nas/_/'gog pa'i bar du mi 'drar 'gro/_/mdor bsdus rgyas dang sangs rgyas kyi/_/bstang bas yongs su ma
[\[10a.7\]]bzung dang /_/dus gsum yon tan med pa dang /_/legs pa'i lam ni rnam gsum la/_/bzung ba'i rnam rtog 'di gcig ste/_/sbyor ba'i rnam pa'i spyod yul can/_/gnyis pa sems dang sems byung rnams/_/'jug pa'i yul can yin bzhed de/_/sems
[\[10b\]]
[\[10b.1\]]mi skye dang byang chub kyi/_/snying po yid la mi byed dang /_/theg pa dman pa yid byed dang /_/rdzogs pa'i byang chub yid mi byed/_/sgom dang sgom pa med pa dang /_/de dag las ni bzlog nyid dang /_/ji bzhin don min rnam rtog pa/_/sgom pa'i lam la shes par
[\[10b.2\]]bya/_/sems can btags pa'i spyod yul dang /_/chos btags pa dang stong min nyid/_/chags dang rab 'byed bdag nyid dang /_/dngos por byed dang theg gsum dang /_/yon ni dag pa ma yin dang /_/spyod pa rnam par 'khrug pa la/_/'dzin par byed pa dang
[\[10b.3\]]por te/_/shes par bya ba bsgrags pa yin/_/sems can btags dang de'i rgyu yi/_/yul can de yis rnam 'joms pas/_/sgom pa'i lam dang 'brel pa yi/_/mi mthun phyogs gzhan rnam pa dgu/_/bdag nyid ji bzhin kun mkhyen ni/_/gsum gyi
[\[10b.4\]]sgrib pa rnam gsum dang /_/zhi lam de bzhin nyid sogs dang /_/mtshungs par ldan dang mi ldan dang /_/mi mnyam sdug bsngal la sogs dang /_/nyon mongs rnams kyi rang bzhin dang /_/gnyis su med dang kun rmongs la/_/rnam par rtog pa tha mar bzhed/_/_
[\[10b.5\]]yams nad 'di rnams zad nas ni/_/yun ring lon nas dbugs phyin ltar/_/rnam pa kun tu 'gro ba yi/_/bde sgrub yon tan phun tshogs kun/_/rgya mtsho che la chu bo bzhin/_/'bras bu mchog gis spa ba yis/_/sems dpa' chen po de la ni/_/rnam
[\[10b.6\]]pa kun du rten par byed/_/stong gsum skye bo nyan thos dang /_/bse ru'i rtogs pa phun tshogs dang /_/byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med la/_/bkod pa'i dge ba dper mdzad nas/_/bsod nams mang po nyid kyis ni/_/sangs rgyas nyid kyi bar med de/_/bar
[\[10b.7\]]chad med pa'i ting nge 'dzin/_/de ni rnam pa kun mkhyen nyid/_/'di yi dmigs pa dngos med de/_/bdag po dran pa yin par bzhed/_/rnam pa zhi nyid 'di la ni/_/rab tu smra rnams brgyud par rgol/_/dmigs pa 'thad dang de yi ni/_/ngo bo nyid nges bzung ba
[\[11a\]]
[\[11a.1\]]dang /_/rnam kun mkhyen nyid ye shes dang /_/dam pa'i don dang kun rdzob dang /_/sbyor dang dkon mchog gsum po dang /_/thabs bcas thub pa'i rtogs pa dang /_/phyin ci log ni lam bcas dang /_/gnyen po mi mthun phyogs dag dang /_/mtshan
[\[11a.2\]]nyid dang ni sgom pa la/_/smra ba rnams kyis log rtog pa/_/rnam pa kun mkhyen nyid rten can/_/rnam pa bcu drug dag tu bzhed/_/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/_skabs lnga pa'o//_//_
[\[11a.3\]]sbyin pa shes rab bar dag dang /_/sangs rgyas la sogs dran dang chos/_/dngos med ngo bo nyid kyis de/_/mthar gyis pa yi bya bar bzhed/_/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa las/_skabs
[\[11a.4\]]drug pa'o//_//sbyin pa la sogs re res kyang /_/zag med chos kun bsdus pa'i phyir/_/thub pa'i skad cig gcig pa yis/_/rtogs pa 'di ni shes par bya/_/ji ltar skyes bus zo chun rgyud/_/rdog thabs gcig gis bskyod pa na/_/thams
[\[11a.5\]]cad cig car 'gul ba ltar/_/skad cig gcig shes de bzhin no/_/gang tshe chos dkar thams cad kyi/_/rang bzhin shes rab pha rol phyin/_/rnam smin chos nyid gnas skabs skyes/_/de tshe skad cig gcig ye shes/_/sbyin la sogs pa'i spyod pa yis/_/_
[\[11a.6\]]chos kun rmi lam 'drar gnas nas/_/chos rnams mtshan nyid med pa nyid/_/skad cig ma ni gcig gis rtogs/_/rmi lam dang ni de mthong nyid/_/gnyis kyi tshul du mi mthong ltar/_/chos rnams gnyis su med pa yi/_/de nyid skad cig gcig gis mthong /_/_

[\[11b\]]

[\[17a.6\]]pa'i gnas skabs ni don du gnyer ba gtsor gyur pa yin pas na de dang lhan cig spyod pa'i sems bskyed pa la don du gnyer ba bstan pa yin te/_de lta na yang byang chub sems dpa' rnams smon lam dang ldan pa'i sems bskyed par 'gyur ba zhes bya ba 'thad par 'gyur
[\[17a.7\]]ba yin no/_/yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub dang gzhan gyi don de yang gang yin zhe na/_de dang de ni mdo bzhin du/_/bsdus dang rgyas pa'i sgo nas brjod/_/ces bya ba gsungs te/_de dang zhes bya ba yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub dang de ni zhes bya ba gzhan gyi don to/_/_
[\[17b\]]
[\[17b.1\]]de la de'i bsdus te bstan pa [#]'di yin te/_shA ri'i bu 'di la byang chub [#]sems dpa' chen po chos thams cad rnam pa thams cad du mngon par [#]'tshang rgya bar 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la brtson par bya'o zhes gang gsungs pa yin no/_/de la de'i rgyas par

[\[18a\]]
[\[18a.1\]]de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa dang po 'dun pa dang ldan pa ni sa lta bu'o/_/shA ri'i bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos thams cad rnam pa thams cad du mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'dod pas

[\[18b.1\]]thams cad shes pa nyid la shes pa dang mthong bas bltas nas 'da' bar 'dod pa dang /_phyir mi ldog pa'i sa la gnas par 'dod pa dang /_lam shes pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par 'dod pa dang rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid rjes su 'thob par 'dod pa'i byang chub [# ]

[\[21b.5\]]gi ngang gis 'jug pa'i phyir dang /_bgrod pa gcig pa nyid ni sa der gtogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams gzhan gyi don gyi bya ba tha mi dad pa'i phyir ro/_/nyi shu gnyis pa chos kyi sku dang ldan pa ni sprin lta bu'o/_/de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod lam bstan

[\[31b\]]
[\[31b.1\]]pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyis sbyor bar mi byed de/_de ci'i slad du zhe na/_gzugs nyid kyang stong pa nyid/_stong pa nyid kyang gzugs so/_/zhes bya bas chos rnams dang /_de'i stong pa nyid phan tshun gyi rang bzhin gcig tu 'dod pas gsungs pa yin no/_/de la
[\[31b.2\]]sngags ni rtag pa'i mtha' bkag la cig shos kyis ni chad pa'i mtha' bkag pa yin no/_/bden pa bzhi'i dbang du mdzad nas sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'i skabs su gnas pa med pa'i dmigs pa'i khyad par ni bcom ldan 'das gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems
[\[31b.3\]]dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/_des gzugs la mi rtag ces gnas mi bgyi'o/_/zhes bya ba nas gzugs la zhi ba'o/_/zhes bgyi bar gnas par mi bgyi'o/_/zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par te/_de ci'i slad du zhe na/_bcom ldan
[\[31b.4\]]'das de ni 'di ltar gzugs mi rtag pa ni gzugs mi rtag pa nyid kyis stong ste/_zhes gsungs pa yin no/_/de la gnas pa ni dngos po la dmigs pa'i sems kyi rten pa'o/_/'dir spyad par bya ste/_gal te re zhig gnas pa med pa tsam gnas par mi bya ba yin na ni med pa'i phyir

[\[31b.6\]]nyid gang lags pa de'ang mi rtag pa nyid ma lags mi rtag pa nyid las gud na yang stong pa nyid ma mchis te zhes bya bas mi rtag pa nyid la sogs pa rnams dang /_de'i stong pa nyid phan tshun de'i bdag nyid kyi rnam pa'i khyad par can dang /[#]de ni 'di ltar gzugs nyid yang dag

[\[32a\]]
[\[32a.1\]]thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyang sangs rgyas nyid yin no/_/byang chub nyid rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa/_rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyang byang chub po zhes bya ba ste/_'dis ni dmigs par bya ba dang /_dmigs pa po mnyam pa nyid kyi

[\[32a.3\]]ro/_/gzugs rtag ces bya ba dang mi rtag ces bya bar mi sbyor ro/_/zhes bya ba la sogs pa yin no/_/chos ni 'dod chags dang bral ba yin pa'i phyir thams cad du 'dod chags dang bral ba yin par bstan pa'i don du gsungs pa ni/_byang chub sems dpa' sbyin
[\[32a.4\]]pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i don du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi spyod do zhes bya ba nas brtsams te/_pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyi don du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa bkag pa dang /_de bzhin du phyir mi ldog pa'i sa la sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i don dang /_sangs

[\[32a.6\]]bzhin nyid dang /_chos kyi dbyings dang /_yang dag pa'i mtha' dang /_lha'i mig yul dang bcas pa dang /_de'i yul phyogs bcu re re zhing gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rnams na sems can rnams kyi 'chi 'pho ba dang skye ba lha'i mig gis
[\[32a.7\]]mthong bar bya'o zhes bya ba'o[#]/_/lha'i rna ba yul dang bcas pa dang /_de'i yul ni bshad ma thag pa'i sems can gyi [#]sgras bsdus pa'o/_/gzhan gyi sems shes pa yul dang bcas pa dang /_de'i yul ni bshad ma thag pa'i sems can rnams kyi sems
[\[32b\]]
[\[32b.1\]]kyis bsdus pa'o/_/sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa dang bcas pa de'i yul ni bshad ma thag pa'i sems can rnams kyi sngon gyi gnas kyis bsdus pa'o/_/rdzu 'phrul gyi yul shes pa yul dang bcas pa'i don du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa bkag pa [# ]

[\[32b.3\]]pa'i nyon mongs pa bsal ba dang /_phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams so so rnams su da ltar bzhugs pa'i [#]sangs rgyas dang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas [#]lha'i rigs rnams srung bar [#]byed pa dang /_mthong ba'i chos nyid la byams pa'i rgyu can gyis las kyi sgrib pa rnam par dag pa dang /_tshegs
[\[32b.4\]]chung ngus gzungs dang ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo mngon du gyur pa dang /_byang chub kyi snying po'i bar du skye ba thams cad du sangs rgyas rnams mnyes par byed pa dang /_chos thams cad nye bar mi dmigs pas phrad pa dang bral ba [#]bkag pa dang /_chos kyi dbyings rjes su
[\[32b.5\]]mi dmigs pa'i phyir de dag gis myur du mngon par byang chub pa bkag pa dang /_sna tshogs par byed pa mi byed pa'i phyir rtogs par bya ba dang rtogs pa po'i chos nye bar mi dmigs pa dang /_chos kyi dbyings la stong pa dang mi stong par sbyor ba [#]bkag pa dang /_
[\[32b.6\]]mig la sogs pa'i khams bco brgyad la stong pa nyid kyis sam/_de la [#]de dag gis sbyor ba bkag pa dang /_nyan thos la sogs pa'i sa las 'da' ba dang /_sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa dang /_sems can yongs su smin par [#]byed pa dang /_myur
[\[32b.7\]]du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir stong pa nyid kyi rnal 'byor mchog tu brjod pa dang /_rtogs pa thams cad la nga rgyal bkag pa dang /_stong pa nyid kyi rnal 'byor la gnas nas snying rje chen po dang byams pa chen po mngon par

[\[34a.1\]]'brang ba gang yin pa de ni dad pas lhag par mos pa zhes brjod de/_dad pa [#]lhag pa nyid kyis na lhag par mos pas rab tu mos pa rab tu [#]phye ba yin pa'i phyir ro/_/dbang po rnon po [#]sngar chos kyis [#]rjes su 'brang bar gyur pa gang yin pa de ni mthong

[\[46a.3\]]nyid mthong ba'i yid la byed pa'i dbang du mdzad pa yin par shes par bya'o/_/gang yang bcom ldan 'das de'i [#]ming de'ang gnas pa ma mchis/_gnas pa [#]dang bral ba ma mchis [#]lags so/_/de ci'i slad du zhe na/_ming de ma mchis pas zhes bya ba de la gnas
[\[46a.4\]]pa ni rgyun 'dra ba'o/_/gnas pa dang bral ba ni rgyun mi 'dra ba'o/_/chen po [#]bcom ldan 'das [#]'di lta ste/_byang chub sems dpa' zhes [#]chos kyi brdar btags pa dang /_chos su gdags pa gang lags pa de'ang zhes bya ba nas/_rgya cher sangs rgyas zhes
[\[46a.5\]]bgyi ba'i ming dang sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams zhes bgyi ba'i ming de yang dge ba'am mi dge ba 'am zhes pa [#]nas dngos po 'am dngos po med pa gang gis kyang brjod du ma mchis so/_/'di lta ste/_dper na/_rmi lam zhes bgyi ba nas sprul pa zhes bgyi ba'i bar gyi ming
[\[46a.6\]]ni gang gis kyang brjod du ma mchis so zhes bya ba nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po de ltar spyod pa ni sems zhum par mi 'gyur 'gyod pa ma mchis la/_mi 'jigs mi dngang skrag par mi 'gyur na rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du nges par 'byung ba lags so zhes bya ba'i

[\[46b.1\]]la sogs pa'i gang zag gi dbye ba yang [#]'di'i dmigs pa la sogs pa rnams kyi khyad par [#]shes par bya ba'i don to/_/rtse mor gyur pa la yang de bzhin du brjod par bya'o/_/dro bar gyur pa ni bden pa bzhi la dmigs pa rnam pa bcu drug dang ldan pa yin la/_drod las ni rtse mor [# ]

[\[47b.1\]]sdug bsngal ba nyid kyang sdug bsngal ba kho na yin te/_dngos po dang stong pa nyid gnyis kyang phan tshun khyab par 'dod pa nyid yin pas nyes pa med do/_/de bzhin du kun 'byung gi bden pa'i dbang du byas nas de'i rnam pa rgyu dang /_kun 'byung ba dang /_rab tu skye ba dang /_

[\[48a.1\]]par ni bcom ldan 'das gal te gzugs la gnas na de gzugs mngon par 'du bgyi ba la spyod kyi/_shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi spyod do zhes bya ba nas brtsams te/_de ci'i slad du zhe na/_mngon par 'du bgyi ba la spyod pa'i byang chub sems

[\[48a.4\]]'khor chos thams cad yongs su ma bzung [#]ba zhes bgyi ba ste zhes bya ba ni rtse mor gyur pa'o/_/de'ang ting nge 'dzin gyi tshogs gzhan dang gzhan thob par byed pas dkyil 'khor yangs pa zhes bya ba ni chos kyi dbyings yangs pa'o/_/mdun du byas pas zhes bya ba ni dmigs pa

[\[48b.5\]]grangs gzhan 'dod pa'i rnam pa'i khyad par dang /_/de ci'i slad du zhe na/_chos thams cad gzung du ma mchis pa dang btang du ma mchis pa gang lags pa de ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lags so zhes bya ba'i 'thad pas gang gsungs pa yin no/_/de la phreng ba can dper

[\[49a.1\]]rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di ni gang gi yin te/_rdzas sam yon tan ni [#]bya ba'am rigs yin zhes bya ba'i don te/_de ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la yongs su brtag par bgyi ste zhes bya ba dang /_ci chos gang zhig yod pa ma yin zhing mi

[\[49a.3\]]pa nyid kyi phyir gzugs med cing mi dmigs so zhes bya ba nas brtsams te/_nang stong pa nyid la sogs pa'i phyir rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bar du med cing mi dmigs so/_/byang chub sems dpa' chen po ni 'di ltar rtog cing sems pa'i [#]tshe/_sems zhum
[\[49a.4\]]pa med cing mi 'jigs mi dngang skrag par mi 'gyur na/_shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ma bral bar shes par bya'o zhes gsungs pa yin no/_/dge ba'i rtsa ba g.yo ba'i rtse mor phyin pas na rtse mo'o/_/rtse mor gyur pa bshad zin to//_//chos thams
[\[49a.5\]]cad ngo bo nyid med pa la dmigs pa nyid kyis bzod pa'i dmigs pa'i khyad par ni/_tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bu gzugs ni gzugs kyi rang bzhin dang bral ba ste zhes bya ba nas brtsams te/_de ci'i slad du [#]zhe na/_tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bu gzugs kyi rang bzhin ni dngos po

[\[49b.6\]]su dag pa dang /_mtshan yongs su dag pa thob par 'gyur ro zhes [#]gsungs pa yin no/_ngan 'gro'i rgyu las yang dag par 'da' ba ni [#]'dod chags dang ldan pa'i sems mi bskyed do zhes bya ba la sogs pa gang gsungs pa yin no/_/yongs su nyams pa las yang dag par 'da'

[\[50a.1\]]spyod kyi zhes bya ba nas brtsams te/_'di snyam du bdag ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod do [#]zhes bgyi bar [#]spyod na dmigs pa la spyod pa ste/_de ni byang chub sems dpa' chen po'i thabs mi mkhas par rig par bgyi'o zhes gang gsungs pa

[\[50a.5\]]na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi spyod do/_/nye bar rtogs pa dang nye bar ma rtogs pa dang /_nye bar rtogs pa yang ma [#]yin la/_nye bar ma rtogs pa yang ma [#]yin pa dang /_nye bar rtogs pa yang ma yin ma rtogs pa yang ma yin na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mi spyod do
[\[50a.6\]]zhes bya ba nas/_de ci'i phyir zhe na/_'di ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni dngos po med pa'i rang bzhin te/_zhes bya ba'i bar dang /_de ltar spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang nye bar gyur pa yin no zhes bya ba'i bar du gang gsungs pa

[\[50b\]]
[\[50b.1\]]nyid kyis chos kyi mchog gi dmigs pa'i khyad par ni chos thams cad skye ba med pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin zhes bya ba nas brtsams te/_ting nge 'dzin brgya lhag dang bcas pa la sogs pa'i [#]ting nge 'dzin dpag tu med pa bstan pas gang gsungs pa yin no/_/ting nge 'dzin gyi
[\[50b.2\]]byed pa rnam pa yin pa nyid kyis na rnam pa'i khyad par ni de la dpa' bar 'gro ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin gang zhe na/_ting nge 'dzin gang gis ting nge 'dzin thams cad kyi spyod yul ston pa ste zhes bya ba nas brtsams te/_ting nge 'dzin thams cad kyi bdag nyid ji lta ba'i byed pa de

[\[69b\]]
[\[69b.1\]]pa yin no/_/bzod pa'i tshogs ni/_gal te sems can thams cad kyis bdag la rdo dang /_dbyug pa dang /_bong ba dang /_khu tshur dang /_lag chas brdeg cing mtshon gyis 'debs kyang de la bdag gis 'khrug pa [#]dang ldan pa'i sems 'ga' tsam yang bskyed par mi

[\[69b.3\]]do zhes bya ba yang dag par nges par sbyor ba dang /_rab tu 'jog pa dang /_ma tshang ba med pa'i don brjod pa rnams kyis gang gsungs pa yin no/_/bsam gtan gyi tshogs ni/_sems can de snyed kho na rang nyid [#]la gnas nas chos 'ga' yang rnam par g.yeng ba dang rnam par [# ]

[\[70a.1\]]ma 'ongs pa'i bde ba nye bar sgrub [#]pa tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang /_bzod pa can spro ba dang ldan pa rtse gcig tu gtod pas ni gcig tu nges pa'i 'bras bu thob [#]pa'i phyir na gcig tu nges pa'i bde ba nye bar sgrub [#]pa bzod pa dang /_brtson 'grus dang /_bsam

[\[70b.1\]]bya ba sems can ma byas [#]rnam par ma byas mngon par 'dus ma byas pa zhes bya ba byed pa'i yul 'gog pa dang /_phung po la sogs pa rnams dang /_bdag dang sems can la sogs pa rnams [#]dang /_rmi lam dang /_sgra brnyan la sogs pa nas de bzhin nyid dang /_ma nor ba de

[\[71a.1\]]byang chub sems dpa' rnams ma bcings ma grol bar shes par bya ba [#]na 'di ni gnas nyid du gsungs pa yin te/_byang chub sems dpa'i snying rjes ni srid pa ji [#]srid du sems can la phan 'dogs la/_shes rab kyis ni der gnas su zin kyang 'khor bar

[\[72a.1\]]pa'i rgyu mtshan bzlog zla skye ba la sogs pa med pa'i phyir ro/_/mtha' ni mthas stong pa nyid yin pa'i phyir mtha' las 'das pa nyid kyis na mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid do/_/mtha' ni cha ste/_de la de dag tshar rnam par gcod pa'i rgyu mtshan gang gis

[\[73a.1\]]par mi rtog pa'i ye shes tsam yin te/_stong pa nyid ces bya ba ni 'ga' yang yod pa ma yin no zhes kha cig zer ro/_/kha cig ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i cha gnyis la gnas pa nyid kyis na cha gcig la dmigs pa ni ma yin no/_/zhes 'dod do/_/la la na re

[\[73a.6\]]na/_ting nge 'dzin gang gis ting nge 'dzin thams cad kyi spyod yul nyams su myong bar byed pa ste/_'di ni dpa' bar 'gro ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to zhes bya ba'i bar ting nge 'dzin brgya rtsa gcig bstan pas gang gsungs pa yin te/_ting nge 'dzin ni mos pa la sogs pa yid la byed
[\[73a.7\]]pa'i rnam pa gsum rab kyi mthar thug par 'gyur ba'i rten yin pas na bsod nams mang po skye ba'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro/_/lam gyi tshogs gsungs pa ni/_rab 'byor gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa chen po ni 'di lta ste/_dran pa nye bar gzhag [#]pa bzhi ste zhes bya ba nas
[\[73b\]]
[\[73b.1\]]brtsams te/_bslab pa las 'da' ba'i g.yeng ba'i gnyen por gnas pa dang 'dug pa la sogs pa'i spyod lam rnams dang /_'gro ba dang /_'ong ba dang /_kun du lta ba dang /_rnam par lta ba'i bya ba rnams la shes bzhin du spyod pa dang /_dbugs 'byung ba dang rngub pa dag la rdza

[\[73b.3\]]rtog [#]pa dang /_de bzhin du phyi rol dang phyi dang nang gi lus la lus kyi rjes su lta bas dran pa nye bar 'jog pa dang /_de lus dang ldan pa'i rnam par rtog pa rnams la yang rnam par mi rtog go zhes bya ba dngos po dang de'i mtshan mar rnam par rtog pa bkag pa yin no/_/dur khrod du zhes bya ba
[\[73b.4\]]ni ro bor ba'i gnas su'o/_/lus 'di nyid ces bya ba ni skye ba 'di nyid pa'o/_/tshul de dang sbyar ro zhes bya ba ni/_shi ba'i ro dang ngo /_/ji ltar nye bar sbyor zhe na/_lus 'di'ang 'di lta bu'i chos can dang 'di lta bu'i rang bzhin can te zhes bya ba ste/_khu ba dang khrag gi gnas skabs

[\[92a.1\]]dang /_len pa por dmigs pas 'jig rten las mi g.yo mi 'phag [#]mi 'da' ba de'i phyir 'jig rten pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa nyid yin pa dang /_'khor gsum yongs su dag pa'i sbyin pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu bsngos pas ni/_'jig rten las sgrol
[\[92a.2\]]bar byed pa dang /_g.yo zhing 'phags la 'da' bar byed pa de'i phyir 'jig rten las 'das pa'i sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yin pa nyid dang /_de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar la'ang brjod par bya'o/_/de la 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyi nges par [#]rnyed pas na 'jig rten las g.yo
[\[92a.3\]]ba'o/_/de thob pa'i thabs nye bar tshol bas na 'phags pa'o/_/de'i bar chad kyi chos yongs su spong bas na 'da' ba'o/_/yang na g.yo ba ni sems bskyed pa'i dus so/_/'phags pa ni nges par 'byed pa'i cha'i dus so/_/'da' ba ni sdug bsngal la chos shes pa'i [#]dus su'o zhes bya ba ni rnam grangs
[\[92a.4\]]gzhan yin no/_/'di las bzlog pas na mi g.yo mi 'phag mi 'da' ba yin par shes par bya'o/_/gang zhig 'jig rten mngon par gsal bar gyur pa yin pa'am/_gang zhig mngon par 'grub par byed pa'am/_gang zhig [#]'jig rten gyis te 'jig rten par mnyam pa'am/_gang zhig [#]'jig rten gyi phyir
[\[92a.5\]]mngon par 'byin pa'am/_gang 'jig rten las nges par mi 'byung ba'am/_gang 'jig rten gyi yin pa'am/_gang 'jig rten du skyed par byed pa de dag ni 'jig rten pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa nyid ces bya ba dang /_gang dag gi [#]'jig rten sgrol pa yin pa'am/_gang gis 'jig rten las sgrol ba'am/_
[\[92a.6\]]gang dag gis 'jig rten la rgal bar byed pa'am/_gang zhig 'jig rten gyi don du mi 'gyur ba'am/_gang zhig 'jig rten las nges par 'byin par byed pa'am/_gang zhig 'jig rten gyi sgrol byed yin pa'am/_gang zhig 'jig rten na sgrol byed yin pa de dag ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i pha
[\[92a.7\]]rol tu phyin pa nyid ces bya ba dang /_'das pa la sogs pa'i 'phags pa'i gang zag thams cad kyi rtogs pa'i rgyu nyid yin pa'i phyir byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun byang chub kyi lam yin pa nyid dang /_'phags pa rnams 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam las nges par skyes pa
[\[92b\]]
[\[92b.1\]]nyid du shes par byed pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa skyed byed yin pa nyid dang /_sems mi zhum pa dang mi skrag pa la sogs pa rnams kyis yid la byed pa dang ma bral ba nyid dang /_de lta yin na ha cang thal ches par brjod pa dang /_de ni yang dag pa'i tshig brjod pa yin te/_de ci'i phyir zhe na/_sems can
[\[92b.2\]]med pa nyid dang [#]/_rang bzhin med pa nyid dang /_stong pa nyid dang /_dben pa nyid dang /[ #]mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang mi rgya ba nyid dang /_de bzhin du gzugs la sogs pa'i chos thams cad nas rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bar la de bzhin du sbyar ba nas/_de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' chen po
[\[92b.3\]]gnas pa 'di dang yid la byed pa 'di dang ma bral lo zhes kho bo smra'o zhes bya ba'i bar gyis yin te/_de ltar nges par 'byung ba brgyad po 'di dag gi [#]nges par 'byung ba'i sgrub pa yin par shes par bya'o/_/go cha'i sgrub pa la sogs pa 'di rnams kyi go rims kyi [#]tshul 'di ni rigs pa nyid yin te/_go bgos pa
[\[92b.4\]]ni 'jug go/_/zhugs pa ni dpung gi tshogs sog go/_/dpung gi tshogs bsags pa ni ma rgyal ba las rgyal ba thob pas nges par 'byung ba yin pa'i phyir ro/_/de ltar byas na/_sems bskyed pa dang gdams ngag dang /_/nges 'byed yan lag rnam bzhi dang /_/sgrub pa yi ni rten gyur pa/_/chos kyi dbyings kyi rang
[\[92b.5\]]bzhin dang /_/dmigs pa dag dang ched dang ni/_/go cha 'jug pa'i bya ba dang /_/tshogs ni nges par 'byung bcas rnams/_/thub pa [#]rnam kun mkhyen pa nyid/_/ces [#]gsungs pa de ni 'dir rjes su 'das pa'i 'brel pa yin par blta bar bya'o/_/sems bskyed pa la sogs pa'i don 'di rnams kyi go rims kyi [#]tshul 'di
[\[92b.6\]]ni rigs pa yin te/_byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i don du gnyer ba ni gdams ngag tshol ba'i phyir dang /_phyin ci ma log pa'i gdams ngag la gnas pa la ni nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa skye ba'i phyir dang /_de nas sgrub pa'i chos gang la brten pa dang /_gang la dmigs pa dang /_ched du bya ba gang yin pa dang /_
[\[92b.7\]]sgrub pa nyid gang yin pa ste rnam pa bzhi yin no/_/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i [#]man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan las rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi dbang du byas pa rab 'byor gyi le'u ste dang po'o/_/[#]rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid bshad zin to//_//[# ]
[\[93a\]]
[\[93a.1\]]da ni lam shes pa nyid brjod par bya ba yin te/_de la re zhig_/lha rnams rung bar bya ba'i phyir/_/'od kyis mog mog por mdzad dang /_/yul nges pa dang khyab pa dang /_/rang bzhin dang ni de yi las/_/brjod par bya'o zhes bya ba ni lhag ma'o/_/_
[\[93a.2\]]de la lha rnams mog mog por mdzad pa nyid ni lha'i ris thams cad kyi 'od de [#]bzhin gshegs pa'i rang bzhin gyi 'od kyis mog mog por mdzad pa gsungs pa gang yin pa ste/_lha rnams kyi 'jig rten skyong ba nyid la sogs pa dang /_bsam gtan la sogs pa thob par
[\[93a.3\]]mngon par rlom pa bsal ba'i don yin no/_/de bsal ba'ang de rnams rung bar bya ba'i don du yin te/_ji skad du de rnams nyid las/_byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos ji ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas par bya/_byang chub sems dpa' sems
[\[93a.4\]]dpa' chen po'i lam shes pa nyid kyi skabs kyi shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gang yin zhes gnas brtan rab 'byor gyis bstan pa nyan pa'i don du smras pa yin no/_/de la rang bzhin gyi 'od ni rnam par smin pa las byung ba'o/_/yul so sor nges pa ni/_ji skad du/_byang chub tu
[\[93a.5\]]sems ma bskyed pa la ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa dang /_bstan pa'i skal ba med pa nyid kyis na lam shes pa nyid ni byang chub sems dpa' kho na'i yin gyi/_nyan thos la sogs pa'i ni ma yin no/_/zhes yul so sor nges pa'i don du gang gsungs pa yin
[\[93a.6\]]no/_/khyab pa ni lam shes pa nyid kyi dbang du byas te/_sems bskyed pa nas brtsams pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni phyogs gcig pa ma yin no zhes khyab pa'i don dang /_go rims [#]dang ldan pa'i gang zag gi khyad par gyi don gyis gsungs pa gang yin pa'o/_/de
[\[93a.7\]]lta yin na[#]/_'on kyang gal te de dag kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed na de dag la rjes su yi rang ste zhes bya ba la sogs pa 'di sngar 'dod chags dang bral ba'i dbang du khyad [#]par 'thad pa yin te/_'dis ni theg pa gsum rnam par gzhag
[\[93b\]]
[\[93b.1\]]pa'i [#]dgongs pa can yin gyi/_mtshan nyid pa ni ma yin no zhes brjod pa yin no/_/rang bzhin ni ji ltar nyan thos la sogs pa'i lam rnams 'bras bu dang lam gyi rtogs pa so sor nges pa de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i lam shes pa ni ma yin te/_rnam pa thams cad du nyon
[\[93b.2\]]mongs pa spong ba yin pa'i phyir ro zhes rang gi ngo bo khyad par du 'phags pa gang gsungs pa yin no/_/byed pa ni ji ltar nyan thos la sogs pa'i lam rnams kyi 'bras bu ni spangs pas rab tu phye ba dang yang dag pa'i mtha' mngon [#]du byed pa de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i de rtogs
[\[93b.3\]]pa ma yin gyi/_'on kyang 'di'i lam shes pa nyid ni sems can yongs su smin pa la sogs pas rab tu phye ba yin no zhes de'i byed pa'i 'bras bu nyid khyad par du 'phags pa'i don gyis gsungs pa gang yin pa'o/_/mog mog por byed pa la sogs pa bshad zin
[\[93b.4\]]to//_//da ni nyan thos kyi lam brjod par bya ba yin pa'i [#]phyir/_lam shes nyid kyi tshul la ni/_/'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi dag gi_/rnam pa mi dmigs sgo nas ni/_/nyan thos lam 'di shes par bya/_/zhes bya ba gsungs pa yin no/_/ji ltar
[\[93b.5\]]zhe na/_gzugs la sogs pa'i phung po rnams dang /_bu ga nam mkha' zhes byar brjod/_/ces bya ba la sogs pa'i khams drug dang /_rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i yan lag rnams [#]rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan par yid la byed pa nyan thos la sogs
[\[93b.6\]]pa'i theg pa 'dod pa dang ma 'dres pa'i don gyis mi rtag pa nyid dang /_sdug bsngal ba nyid dang /_bdag med pa nyid dang /_zhi ba nyid dang /_nad nyid dang /_'bras nyid dang /_zug rngu nyid dang /_sdig pa nyid dang /_pha rol nyid dang /_'jig pa'i chos can nyid dang /_g.yo
[\[93b.7\]]ba nyid dang /_rab tu 'jig pa nyid dang /[#]'go nad nyid dang /_'tshe ba nyid ces bya ba ni sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung gi bden pa'i rnam pa rnams mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis yid la byed pa'o/_/de la mi rtag pa nyid nas zhi ba nyid ces bya ba'i bar ni sdug bsngal gyi bden
[\[94a\]]
[\[94a.1\]]pa'i rnam pa'o/_/nad nyid ces bya ba nas sdig pa nyid ces bya ba'i bar ni kun 'byung gi bden pa'i rnam pa'o/_/pha rol nyid dang 'jig pa'i chos can nyid ces bya ba ni de dag nyid so so la yang [#]byung ba'i rnam pa'o/_/g.yo ba nyid dang rab tu 'jig pa nyid
[\[94a.2\]]ces bya ba ni de dag nyid so so la 'dod chags dang bral ba'i rnam pa'o/_/'jig [#]pa nyid dang 'go nad nyid dang 'tshe ba nyid ces bya ba ni de dag nyid so so la 'gog pa'i rnam pa'o/_/de ltar byas na [#]'phags pa nyan thos rnams yid byung ba dang 'dod chags dang bral ba dang [#]'gog pa'i

[\[94a.4\]]dang 'phags pa'i lam ni mi rtag pa yin yang zag pa med pa nyid kyis 'phags pa rnams dang mi mthun pa [#]yin pa'i phyir 'di sdug bsngal nyid du thal bar mi 'gyur ro/_/bdag med pa nyid ces bya ba ni bdag gzhan gyis stong pa'i phyir ro/_/zhi ba nyid ces bya ba ni rang nyid
[\[94a.5\]]bdag ma yin pa'i phyir ro/_/nad nyid ces bya ba ni 'bras bu'i sa bon dang 'dra bar rgyu'i rtsa bar 'gyur ba nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/'bras nyid ces bya ba ni sdug bsngal kun 'byung ba nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/zug rngu nyid ces bya ba ni sdug bsngal gyi rkyen nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/_

[\[94a.7\]]can nyid yin pa'i phyir te/_yid byung ba'i dmigs par yang 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go/_/g.yo ba nyid ces bya ba ni rang gi ngo bor gnas pa med pa nyid kyi phyir ro/_/rab tu 'jig pa nyid ces bya ba ni rgyu la ltos [#]pa med par rang bzhin gyis 'jig pa nyid yin pa'i phyir te/_

[\[94b.1\]]'dod chags dang bral ba'i dmigs par yang 'gyur ro zhes bya ba yin no/_/'jig [#]pa nyid ces bya ba ni 'di dang gzhan gyi gnod pa'i gnas su gyur pa nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/'go ba'i nad nyid ces bya ba ni srin po la sogs pa'i gnod pas glags thob pa nyid kyis so/_/_
[\[94b.2\]]'tshe ba nyid ces bya ba ni 'byung ba chen po 'khrugs pa dang thog 'bab pa la sogs pa'i gnod pa'i gnas su gyur pa nyid yin pa'i phyir te/_'gog pa'i dmigs par yang 'thad pa yin no zhes bya ba'o/_/yid la byed pa de rnams nyid kyis ma rig pa 'gog pa la bdag med
[\[94b.3\]]pa nyid dang /_zhi ba nyid dang /_dben pa nyid ces bya bar yid la byed pa gsum ni 'gog pa'i bden pa'i rnam pa'o/_/nges par 'byung ba'i rnam pa bzhi ni gang gi phyir stong pa nyid dang /_mtshan ma med pa nyid dang /_smon pa med pa nyid dang /_mngon par 'du byed pa med

[\[94b.5\]]pa zhes bya ba ni lam gyi rnam pa ste/_de rnams ni mya ngan las 'das pa'i grong khyer thob par byed pa'i don gyis so/_/de dag nyid kyis mi dmigs pa'i tshul du sbyin pa la sogs pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa zhes bya ba ni rigs pa'i rnam pa ste/_ma lus par

[\[95a.1\]]cing mi dmigs pa nyid kyis so zhes bya ba ni sgrub pa'i rnam pa ste/_rtogs par byed pas na sgrub pa yin pas so/_/de ci'i phyir zhe na/_byang chub kyi sems dang yongs su bsngo ba'i sems dag ni sems ma yin pa nyid kyis dang /_sems ma yin
[\[95a.2\]]pa'ang sems ma yin par yongs su bsngo ba ni mi 'thad pa nyid dang /_'di ltar sems ma yin pa gang yin pa de ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa yin [#]la/_bsam gyis mi khyab pa gang yin pa de'ang sems ma yin te/_de ltar so sor rtog pa mngon par zhen pa med pa'i shes rab
[\[95a.3\]]kyi pha rol tu phyin pa nyid yin no zhes bya ba ni nges par 'byin pa'i rnam pa ste/_mngon par zhen pa med par 'gro ba ni nges par 'byin pas so/_/nyan thos kyi lam gyi bden pa bzhi la dmigs pa'i rnam pa bcu drug gi rnam par gzhag [#]pa bshad zin to//_//de dag sngon
[\[95a.4\]]du 'gro ba can yin pa'i nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa de dag brjod par bya ba yin pa des na/_'phags pa nyan thos lam la ni/_/gzugs sogs phung po stong pa'i phyir/_/stong pa nyid rnams dbyer med pas/_/dro ba zhes bya ba gsungs te/_drod ni kau shi ka
[\[95a.5\]]gzugs ni gzugs kyis stong ngo /_/de bzhin du tshor ba la sogs pa dang /_gzugs kyi stong pa nyid gang yin pa dang /_tshor ba la sogs pa'i stong pa nyid gang yin pa de ni gnyis su med cing gnyis su byar med de zhes bya ba la sogs pa gang gsungs pa yin no/_/_

[\[95a.7\]]gang gsungs pa yin no/_/de la rtag la sogs tshul gyis/_/gnas pa bkag pas bzod pa rnams/_/zhes bya ba ni dmigs pa'i tshul gyis gzugs rtag ces bya ba dang mi rtag ces bya bar gnas par mi bya'o/_/gzugs bde zhes bya ba nas smon pa med ces bya ba'i bar du

[\[95b.1\]]gnas par mi bya'o zhes bya ba la sogs pas gang gsungs pa yin no/_/sa bcu dag la brtsams nas ni/_/mi gnas rgyas par bstan pa yis/_/chos kyi mchog tu 'gyur bshad de/_/zhes bya ba ni byang chub sems dpa' chen pos sa dang po la dmigs pa'i tshul

[\[95b.6\]]skad la sogs pa ni shes par rung gi gnas brtan rab 'byor gyis bshad pa'i don ni shes par mi rung ngo zhes gsungs pa yin no/_/gnod sbyin rnams kyi gnod sbyin gyi skad dang /_gnod sbyin gyi tshig dang /_gnod sbyin gyis smras pa dang /_gnod sbyin gyis rab tu bsnyad pa
[\[95b.7\]]gang yin pa de dag ni zhes bya ba [(]ya [,]la [)]sogs pa gsungs pa gang yin pa de la gnod sbyin gyi skad ces bya ba [#]de dag gi rang gi brdas rtogs par byed pa'o/_/tshig ces bya ba ni skad kyi tshogs so/_/smras pa zhes bya ba ni ji srid kyis brjod par 'dod pa'i don yongs su rdzogs par
[\[96a\]]
[\[96a.1\]]'gyur ba'i ngag ces bya ba'i don to/_/rab tu bsnyad pa zhes bya ba ni gtam gyi lan [#]de dang de dag tu dris pa dang lan btab pa'o/_/gang yin pa de dag ni zhes bya ba ni sngon nye bar thob [#]pa rnams so/_/de ni shes par rung gi/_/gnas brtan 'phags pa rab
[\[96a.2\]]'byor shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'chad pa dang /_rab tu brjod pa dang /_ston pa dang /[#]nye bar ston pa zhes bya ba de la gsol ba btab nas ston pa ni 'chad pa'o/_/dris nas lan du smra ba ni rab tu brjod pa'o/_/gnyis po de nyid gdul bya rmongs pa rnams kyi dbang du byas
[\[96a.3\]]nas 'chad pa ni ston pa'o/_/bag med pa rnams kyi dbang du byas nas ni nye bar 'ongs nas ston pa nyid kyis nye bar ston pa yin no/_/lha'i bu dag 'di ltar 'dir yi ge gcig kyang ma brjod de [#]zhes bya ba nas brtsams pas rab tu ston pa dang nyan pa bkag pa'i phyir te/_shes
[\[96a.4\]]rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub dag ni sprul pa dang /_rmi lam dang /_sgra brnyan dang /_sgyu ma'i dpe rnams kyis yi ge med pa yin pa'i phyir rab tu brjod pa dang nyan pa med pas so zhes bya'o/_/ji ltar na chos ston pa zhes bya ba yang yin la rab
[\[96a.5\]]tu mi brjod pa'ang yin zhe na/_chos ston pa'i 'bras bu thob pa'i rgyu nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/sangs rgyas kyi smon lam grub pa'i yang phyir te/_chos ston pa ni brjod pa'i rang bzhin yin pas rnam par g.yeng ba chen por 'gyur ba yin la/_rnam par g.yeng ba'ang rgyud mi zad
[\[96a.6\]]par 'khrug par byed pa yin par dgongs nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sngon byang chub sems dpar gyur pas bdag gis sangs rgyas nyid thob nas yid bzhin gyi nor bu lta bu brjod pa med par yang sems can gyi don byed nus par gyur cig ces de ltar smon lam btab pa yin
[\[96a.7\]]no/_/tshig tu smra ba med par don ston pa'ang rung ba yin no/_/zhes bstan pa'i phyir/_gang gang don ni [#]gang gang la/_/ji lta ji ltar nyan 'dod pa/_/de de la don de dang de/_/sgra med kyang de de ltar snang /_/zhes gsungs so/_/de la ye shes zab mo ni 'di yin te/_kye ma gnas
[\[96b\]]
[\[96b.1\]]brtan rab 'byor 'di ni gsal bar byed pa ste/_zab pa bas kyang shin tu zab pa ston pa phra ba bas kyang shin tu phra ba la 'jug pa'o zhes gang gsungs pa yin no/_/de la gnas brtan rab 'byor gyis nye bar bstan pa'i don mi rig pa ni shes pa zab pa yin la/_yi ge gcig kyang

[\[139b.2\]]ma gsum pas bsdus pa ni/_yang skyes bu rgas shing nyam [#]chung ba'i dpes lhan cig byed pa'i rgyu shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang thabs la mkhas pas yongs su bzung ba dang yongs su ma bzung bar bstan pas 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i mtha' gcig tu ltung ba
[\[139b.3\]]dang mi ltung bar ston pa'i don la sogs pa gang gsungs pa yin no/_/ro myang ba med pa'i khyad par lam gyi skad cig ma bzhi pas bsdus pa ni yang chos thams cad ngo bo nyid med pa'i phyir chos thams cad la mchog tu 'dzin pa med pa dang /_'dod pa med pa nyid kyis dge ba'i rtsa
[\[139b.4\]]ba bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sngo [#]bar byed pa [#]brten par bya ba la sogs pa nyid du gang gsungs pa yin no/_/bshad ma thag pa'i tshig lhug pas gsungs pa'i don gang yin pa de tshigs su bcad pas bsdus pa ni 'di yin te/_bsam mi khyab dang
[\[139b.5\]]mi mnyam dang /_/gzhal dang bgrang las yang dag 'das/_/'phags pa kun sdud mkhas pa yis/_/rig bya thun mong min shes nyid/_/shes myur bri dang gang med dang /_/sgrub dang yang dag 'grub pa dang /_/dmigs pa rten [#]dang bcas pa dang /_/mtha' dag
[\[139b.6\]]pa dang yongs 'dzin dang /_/ro myang med dang khyad par ni/_/bcu drug bdag nyid ces [#]bya ste/_/gang gis lam 'di gzhan dag las/_/khyad du 'phags pas [#]khyad par lam/_/zhes bya'o[#]/_/khyad par gyi mtshan nyid bshad zin to//_//byed pa'i mtshan nyid
[\[139b.7\]]brjod par bya ba yin pas/_phan dang bde dang skyob pa dang /_/mi rnams kyi ni skyabs dag dang /_/gnas dang dpung gnyen gling dang ni/_/yongs 'dren pa zhes bya ba dang /_/lhun gyis grub dang theg gsum gyi/_/'bras bu mngon du mi byed bdag_/tha ma rten gyi mdzad
[\[140a\]]
[\[140a.1\]]pa ste/_/'di ni byed pa'i mtshan nyid yin/_/zhes bya ba gsungs pa yin no/_/de la phan pa'i byed pa ni sems can rnams 'gro ba rgyud lnga las yongs su bton cing mya ngan las 'das [#]pa la rab tu 'god pa'i phyir 'jig rten la phan par zhugs [#]pas
[\[140a.2\]]ma 'ongs pa'i phan pas bsdus pa'i don gyis gang gsungs pa yin no/_/bde ba'i byed pa ni sems can rnams sdug bsngal ba dang yid mi bde ba dang 'khrug pa rnams las yongs su bkrol zhing mya ngan las 'das pa la rab tu 'god pa'i phyir 'jig rten la bde bar [#]yang
[\[140a.3\]]dag par zhugs pas tshe 'di'i bde bas bsdus pa'i don gyis gang gsungs pa yin no/_/skyob pa'i byed pa ni byang chub sems dpa' 'khor ba na yod pa'i sdug bsngal gang ci yang rung ba las skyob cing yang mi skye bar byed pa'i chos ston pa'i phyir 'jig rten gyi [#]skyob pa yin pa nyid kyis
[\[140a.4\]]rnam par smin pa med pa'i chos la 'jog pa'i don gyis gang gsungs pa yin no/_/skyabs kyi byed pa ni sems can skye ba la sogs pa'i chos can rnams phung po ma lus pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su rab tu 'god pa'i phyir 'jig rten gyi skyabs su gyur pa nyid kyis
[\[140a.5\]]gtan du phan pa la zhugs pa'i don gyis gang gsungs pa yin no/_/gnas kyi byed pa ni chos thams cad 'dre ba med pa dang /_'brel pa med pa dang /_skye ba med pa dang /_'gag pa med par [#]ston pa'i phyir gnas su gyur pa nyid kyis sdug bsngal gyi rgyu las bzlog pa'i don
[\[140a.6\]]gyis gang gsungs pa yin no/_/dpung gnyen gyi byed pa ni gang chos thams cad kyi pha rol gang yin pa de ni chos thams cad ma yin no/_/de ci'i phyir zhe na/_gzugs la sogs pa'i pha rol na gzugs la sogs pa'i rnam par rtog pa gang yang med
[\[140a.7\]]do zhes chos ston pa'i phyir/_dpung gnyen du gyur pa nyid kyis 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa mnyam pa nyid du rtogs pa nye bar bsgrub [#]pa'i don gyis gang gsungs pa yin no/_/gling gi byed pa ni gzugs la sogs pa'i sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha' yongs su chad
[\[140b\]]
[\[140b.1\]]pas chus yongs su bskor ba'i skams [#]dang chos mthun par sred pa zad pa dang /_'dod chags dang bral ba dang /_'gog pa dang /_mya ngan las 'das pa ston pa'i phyir gling du gyur pa nyid kyis rang dang gzhan gyi don rtogs pa'i rten gyi ngo bor gyur pa nye bar bsgrub [#]pa'i don gyis
[\[140b.2\]]gang gsungs pa yin no/_/yongs su 'dren pa'i byed pa ni gzugs la sogs pa'i chos thams cad skye ba med pa dang /_'gag pa med pa dang /_kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang /_rnam par byang ba med pa'i phyir chos yang dag par ston pa las yongs su 'dren
[\[140b.3\]]par gyur pa nyid kyis gzhan gyi don sgrub pa la 'jug pa'i don gyis gang gsungs pa yin no/_/lhun gyis grub pa'i byed pa ni/_rab 'byor gzugs ni nam mkha'i ngang tshul can zhes bya ba la sogs pa dang /_gzugs kyi stong pa nyid ni 'gro ba med pa ste/_de ni mi 'gro
[\[140b.4\]]mi 'ong ngo zhes bya ba nas brtsams te/_rab 'byor chos thams cad ni mngon par 'du byed pa med pa'i ngang tshul can te/_de dag ni ngang tshul de las mi 'da' zhes bya ba'i bar gyis thams cad shes pa'i dbang du mdzad nas chos ston par mdzad pa nyid kyis kyang sems can
[\[140b.5\]]gyi don la lhun gyis grub par 'jug pa nye bar bsgrub [#]pa'i don gyis gang gsungs pa yin no[#]/_/thams cad shes pa'i dbang du mdzad pa'i byed pa thams cad [#]mya ngan las 'das par ston pa'i don gyis gang gsungs pa yin par shes par bya'o/_/theg pa gsum gyi nges
[\[140b.6\]]par 'byung zhing de'i 'bras bu mngon du mi [#]byed pa ni/_rab 'byor chos thams cad mi skye mi 'gag pa dang /_kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang /_rnam par byang ba med pa'i ngang tshul can zhes bya ba nas brtsams te/_rab 'byor chos thams cad [#]mi g.yo ba'i ngang
[\[140b.7\]]tshul can te zhes bya ba'i bar gyis lam shes pa'i chos ston pa nyid kyis theg pa ji lta ba bzhin nges par 'byung ba dang de mngon du mi byed pa nye bar bsgrub [#]pa'i don gyis gang gsungs pa yin no/_/rten gyi byed pa ni/_rab 'byor chos thams cad ni gzugs kyi ngang tshul can te zhes
[\[141a\]]
[\[141a.1\]]bya ba nas brtsams te/_rab 'byor chos thams cad ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi ngang tshul can zhes bya ba [#]chos thams cad rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du ston pa nyid kyis byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi [#]don du gang
[\[141a.2\]]gsungs pa yin no/_/byed pa'i mtshan nyid bshad zin to//_//ngo bo nyid kyi mtshan nyid brjod par bya ba yin pas/_nyon mongs rtags dang mtshan ma dang /_/mi mthun phyogs dang gnyen po dag_/dben dang dka' dang nges pa dang /_/ched du bya dang mi dmigs dang /_/_

[\[141a.4\]]bzhed pa yin/_/zhes bya ba gsungs pa yin no/_/bcu drug gi bdag nyid yin zhes ji ltar brjod ce na/_nyon mongs pa las dben pa'i ngo bo nyid ni/_'dod chags dang /_zhe sdang dang /_gti mug rnam par bsal bas dben pa'i rang bzhin du gyur pa nyid du gang gsungs pa
[\[141a.5\]]yin no/_/de'i rtags kyis dben pa'i ngo bo nyid ni 'dod chags la sogs pa'i rtags kyis dben par gang gsungs pa yin no/_/de'i mtshan mas dben pa'i ngo bo nyid ni nyon mongs pa'i mtshan mas dben pa'i rang bzhin du gang gsungs pa yin no/_/de la rtags ni lus la sogs
[\[141a.6\]]pa'i gnas ngan len no[#]/_/mtshan ma ni tshul bzhin ma yin pa'i yid la byed pa'o/_/mi mthun pa dang gnyen po'i phyogs dag gis dben pa'i ngo bo nyid ni/_de bzhin du 'dod chags dang /_'dod chags med pa dang /_zhe sdang dang /_zhe sdang med pa dang /_gti mug dang /_

[\[141b.1\]]pa'i phyir de dang 'brel pa med pa nyid nye bar bzung nas sems can thams cad yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i [#]go cha bya dka' ba nyid kyis shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgom pa bya dka' [#]ba'i don du ston pas gang gsungs pa yin no/_/nges pa'i ngo bo nyid ni de ltar go cha

[\[141b.4\]]so zhes bya bas bsgom par bya ba dang /_sgom pa po dang /_bsgom pa mi dmigs pa'i rnam par bsgom [#]pa nas brtsams te/_bcom ldan 'das rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid bsgom [#]pa 'di ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa sgom pa rnam par bsgom [#]pa ma lags so zhes
[\[141b.5\]]bya bas thams cad shes pa nyid kyi rnam par bsgom [#]pa nyid du gang gsungs pa yin no/_/mngon par zhen pa med pa'i ngo bo nyid ni/_rab 'byor shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'di la phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos yongs su brtag
[\[141b.6\]]par bya'o zhes bya bas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la mngon par ma zhen par yongs su rtog pa nas brtsams te/_'di bshad pa la mi dngang ba la sogs pa rnams kyis [#]lam shes pa'i rnam pa bsgom pa nyid du gang gsungs pa yin no/_/dmigs pa'i ngo bo nyid ni/_bcom

[\[142a.1\]]sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zab mo 'di la rtog pa yin no zhes bya ba'i bar gyis rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i rnam par bsgom [#]pa nye bar dgod pa dang /_gzugs nas rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bar la yang rtog

[\[142a.5\]]la sogs pa gang yin pa de ji ltar yin zhe na/_gzugs nyid rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid do/_/rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid gzugs so zhes bya bas de dag phan tshun gyi ngo bo'i zab pa nyid dang /_de ci'i phyir zhe na/_de dag gi de bzhin nyid dag gnyis su
[\[142a.6\]]byar med pa nyid du gang gsungs pa yin no/_/gal te de lta yin na/_'o na chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba ji ltar 'thad ce na/_sangs rgyas dang rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi de bzhin nyid dag gnyis su med cing gnyis su byar med pa nyid kyis chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i
[\[142a.7\]]don du thugs las chung ba nyid kyi rgyu nyid yin par gsungs te dmigs par bya ba dang /_dmigs par byed pa'i dbye ba med pa nyid yin no zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go/_/'jig rten thams cad dang mi mthun pa'i ngo bo nyid ni/_lha'i bu dag nam mkha' zab pa'i phyir chos 'di zab po
[\[142b\]]
[\[142b.1\]]zhes bya ba nas brtsams te/_rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bar du bzung ba'i slad du bstan pa ma lags/_mi bzung ba'i slad du bstan pa ma lags so/_/bcom ldan 'das 'jig rten ni 'dzin pa la spyod do zhes bya bas 'jig rten thams cad dang mi mthun pa

[\[142b.3\]]gzugs la sogs pa thams cad la ye shes kyi chos thogs pa med pa nyid du gang gsungs pa yin no/_/gzhi med pa'i ngo bo nyid ni gzugs la sogs pa'i rten [#]mi dmigs pa nas brtsams te/_shes pa dang shes bya mnyam pa nyid kyi don gyis gang gsungs pa yin no/_/'gro
[\[142b.4\]]ba med pa'i ngo bo nyid ni/_thams cad mkhyen pa gsum po mtha' dag kyang skyed par byed pa'i dbang du byas te/_shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom [#]pa las gnas brtan rab 'byor dper byas te[#]/_ji ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i de bzhin nyid gang yin pa de ni ma 'ongs ma
[\[142b.5\]]song ba de bzhin du gnas brtan rab 'byor gyi de bzhin nyid kyang ma 'ongs ma song bas na/_gnas brtan rab 'byor ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i rjes su skyes so zhes bya ba la sogs pa gang gsungs pa yin no/_/chos rnams kyi de bzhin nyid kyang de bzhin no zhes bya ba ni rdzas
[\[142b.6\]]su 'dod pa gzugs la sogs pa rnams kyi spyi'i chos nyid do/_/gnas pa'i de bzhin nyid ces bya ba ni rgyun gyi chos nyid do/_/mi 'gyur zhing rnam par rtog pa med pa'i de bzhin nyid ces bya ba ni sgrub pa'i chos khyad par du 'gro ba dang de la rnam par rtog pa med pa'i chos nyid
