[\[204a.1\]]ba rnams bcom pas na sku rgyas pa dang /_yang srid pa dang rjes su 'brel pa zad pas na sku shin tu grims pa dang /_rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i yan lag dang nying lag legs par ston par mdzad pas na yan lag dang nying lag shin tu rnam par [(]'byis [,]'byes [) ]
[\[204a.2\]]pa dang /_gzigs pa rnam par dag pas na gzigs pa rab rib med cing rnam par dag pa dang /_tshul khrims [#]phun sum tshogs pa'i slob ma mnga' bas na dku zlum pa dang /_'khor ba'i skyon rab tu sbyangs pas na dku skabs phyin pa dang /_nga rgyal gyi dreg [#]pa bcom pas [#]na dku
[\[204a.3\]]ma rnyongs pa dang /_chos zad pa rnam par bzlog par mdzad pas na phyal phyang nge ba dang /_chos zab mo mngon du mdzad pas na lte ba zab pa dang /_mthun par 'dzin pa'i slob ma mnga' bas na lte ba g.yas su 'khyil ba dang /_kun nas mdzes pa'i slob ma'i tshogs mnga' bas na kun nas
[\[204a.4\]]mdzes pa dang /_thugs mchog tu gtsang bas na kun du spyod pa gtsang ba dang /_chos 'dul ba nag po ston pa dang bral bas na sku la sme ba dang gnag bag med pa dang /_shing bal dang 'dra bar yang ba'i lus thob par byed pa'i chos ston par mdzad pas na phyag shing bal ltar 'jam pa
[\[204a.5\]]dang /_rang gi skye bo dang skye bo phal po che la snyoms par byas pas dge sbyong chen po brnyes pas na phyag gi ri mo mdangs yod pa dang /_mchog tu zab cing brtan par gnas pas na phyag gi ri mo zab pa dang /_rgya chen po la bzod pa'i chos ston par mdzad pas na phyag gi ri mo ring ba dang /_
[\[204a.6\]]shin tu rlabs po che ma yin pa'i bslab pa'i gzhi 'cha' bar mdzad pas na zhal ha cang mi ring ba dang /_'jig rten thams cad gzugs brnyan dang 'dra bar ston pas na zhal la gzugs kyi [#]gzugs brnyan snang ba dang /_'jam pa sngon du btang nas 'dul bas na ljags mnyen pa dang /_
[\[204a.7\]]yon tan phra mo'i tshogs dang ldan pas na ljags srab pa dang /_byis pa'i skye bo chags pa can rnams gting dpag dka' ba'i chos kyis 'dul bas na ljags dmar ba dang /_glang po che'i nga ro dang /_'brug gi sgra rnams la bsnyems [#]pa mi mnga' bas [#]glang po che dang 'brug gi
[\[204b\]]
[\[204b.1\]]sgra dbyangs dang ldan pa dang /_snyan zhing mnyen la 'jam pas smra ba'i slob ma mnga' bas na gsung [#]snyan zhing mnyen la 'jam pa dang /_srid pa kun tu sbyor ba bsdams pas na mche ba zlum pa dang /_skye bo rnon pos [#]'dul ba la mkhas pas na mche ba rno ba dang /_chos 'dul ba mchog tu dkar
[\[204b.2\]]bas na mche ba dkar ba dang /_sa'i cha mnyam [#]pa la zhugs [#]pas na mche ba mnyam pa dang /_mngon par rtogs pa rim gyis ston par mdzad pas na mche ba byin gyis phra ba dang /_shes rab kyi ri bo mthon po la bzhugs [#]pas na shangs mtho ba dang /_gdul bya'i skye bo gtsang ma yid [#]ches pas
[\[204b.3\]]na shangs gtsang ba dang /_sangs rgyas kyi chos mchog tu yangs pa dang ldan pas na spyan yangs pa dang /_sems can gyi tshogs bsags pas na rdzi ma stug pa dang /_lha dang lha ma yin dang mi'i na chung ltar [#]mig dkar nag 'byes shing pad+ma'i 'dab ma rangs pa lta bu dang ldan pas [#]mchog
[\[204b.4\]]rnams kyis mngon par bstod pas na spyan dkar nag 'byes shing pad+ma'i 'dab ma rangs pa lta bu dang /_rtag tu yangs pa ston pas na smin tshugs ring ba dang /_'jam pos 'dul ba la mkhas pas na smin ma 'jam pa dang /_skyon kun nas mkhyen pas na smin ma'i spu mnyam pa dang /_
[\[204b.5\]]dge ba'i rtsa ba nye bar snum pas rgyud snum par gyur pa'i skye bo rnams 'dul bas na smin ma snum pa dang /_mchog tu rgyas shing ring ba'i phyag mnga' bas [#]na phyag rgyas shing ring ba dang /_nyon mongs pa'i g.yul las rnam par rgyal bas na snyan mnyam pa dang /_ma nyams [#]pa'i sems can gyi rgyud
[\[204b.6\]]'dul bar mdzad pas na snyan gyi dbang po ma nyams pa dang /_blta bar bya ba [#]thams cad rnam par spang bas [#]na dpral ba legs par 'byes pa dang /_dge sbyong dang bram ze dang phas kyi rgol ba rnams rab tu bcom pas na dpral ba'i dbyes che ba dang /_smon lam gyi mchog [#]tu yongs su rdzogs
[\[204b.7\]]pas na yan lag gi mchog shin tu rgyas pa dang /_yul gyi bung ba'i dga' ba rnam par bzlog pas na dbu skra bung ba ltar gnag pa dang /_mthong ba dang sgom pas spang bar bya ba'i bag la nyal spangs pas na dbu skra stug pa dang /_blo 'jam pos bstan pa'i snying po mngon par mkhyen pas na dbu skra
[\[205a\]]
[\[205a.1\]]'jam pa dang /_rtag tu ma 'khrugs pa'i thugs mnga' bas na dbu skra ma 'dzings pa dang /_rtag tu ma brlang [#]ba'i gsung mnga' bas na dbu skra mi bshor ba dang /_byang chub kyi yan lag gi me tog dri zhim pos skye bo rnams mthun par bsgrubs [#]pas na dbu skra
[\[205a.2\]]dri zhim pa dang /_phyag dang zhabs kyi mthil dpal be'u dang bkra shis dang g.yung drung 'khyil bas brgyan pa yin no/_/mdo'i tshig lhug pa [#]bsdu bar bya ba'i don du tshig le'ur byas pa tshigs su bcad pa 'di yin te/_thub pa'i sen mo zangs mdog dang /_/mdog snum mtho dang
[\[205a.3\]]sor mo rnams/_/zlum rgyas byin gyis phra ba dang /_/rtsa mi mngon pa [#]mdud pa med/_/long bu mi mngon zhabs mnyam dang /_/seng ge glang chen bya dang ni/_/khyu mchog stabs gshegs g.yas phyogs dang /_/mdzes gshegs drang dang 'khril bag chags/_/byi dor byas
[\[205a.4\]]'dra rim par 'tsham/_/gtsang dang 'jam dang dag pa'i sku/_/mtshan ni yongs su rdzogs pa dang /_/sku yi kho lag yangs shing bzang /_/gom snyoms pa dang spyan gnyis ni/_/dag dang gzhon sha can nyid dang /_/sku zhum med dang rgyas pa dang /_/shin tu [(]grams [,]grims [) ]
[\[205a.5\]]pa'i sku nyid dang /_/yan lag shin tu rnam 'byes dang /_/gzigs pa sgrib med dag pa dang /_/dku zlum skabs phyin ma rnyongs [#]dang /_/phyang nge ba dang lte ba ni/_/zab dang g.yas phyogs 'khyil ba dang /_/kun nas lta na sdug pa dang /_/kun spyod gtsang dang sku la ni/_/sme ba
[\[205a.6\]]gnag bag med pa dang /_/phyag ni shing bal ltar 'jam dang /_/phyag ris [#]mdangs yod zab ring dang /_/zhal ni ha cang mi ring dang /_/mchu ni bim pa ltar dmar dang /_/ljags mnyen pa dang srab pa dang /_/dmar dang 'brug gi sgra nyid dang /_/gsung mnyen 'jam dang mche ba
[\[205a.7\]]zlum/_/rno dang dkar dang mnyam pa dang /_/byin gyis phra dang shangs mtho dang /_/mchog tu gtsang ba nyid dang ni/_/spyan yangs pa dang rdzi ma stug_/pad+ma'i 'dab ma 'dra ba dang /_/smin tshugs ring dang 'jam pa dang /_/snum dang spu ni mnyam pa dang /_/phyag ring rgyas dang snyan

[\[205b.1\]]mnyam dang /_/nyams pa rnam par spangs pa dang /_/dpral ba legs par 'byes pa dang /_/dbyes che ba dang dbu rgyas dang /_/dbu skra bung ba ltar gnag dang /_/stug dang 'jam dang ma 'dzings dang /_/mi bshor dri zhim skyes bu yi/_/yid ni 'phrog par byed pa dang /_/dpal

[\[205b.3\]]par 'gyur te/_des na dang por [#]ma gsungs so/_/sprul pa'i sku gang zhe na/[#]gang gis srid pa ji srid par/_/'gro la phan pa sna tshogs dag_/mnyam du mdzad pa'i sku de ni/_/thub pa'i sprul sku rgyun mi chad[#]/_/de bzhin 'gro la ji srid 'di'i/_/las kyang rgyun mi
[\[205b.4\]]'chad par 'dod/_/ces gsungs so/_/des na 'di phan chad ni 'bras bu'i gnas skabs rnam pa thams cad legs par yongs su rdzogs pa'i chos kyi sku thob pa ni 'khor ba ji srid par phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams su sprul pa rnams kyis lhun gyis grub cing rgyun mi
[\[205b.5\]]'chad par sems can gyi don sna tshogs pa 'jug par byed pa'i sgo nas gnas yongs su gyur pa'i phrin las kyi dbang du mdzad do/_/bcom ldan 'das rmi lam lta bu dngos po med pa dang /_dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid dang /_rang gi mtshan nyid kyi [#]stong pa'i chos rnams la dge ba dang /_

[\[206a\]]
[\[206a.1\]]ji lta ba bzhin du nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa'i gnyen po nye bar mi dmigs pa shes par byed pa'i don can dang /_dka' ba byed pa rnams kyi chos rnam par gzhag par [#]bya dka' ba ngo mtshar che ba nyid du gang [#]gsungs pa yin no/_/'di bzhin 'di

[\[206a.7\]]chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dag bsams bzhin du sems can dmyal ba chen po rnams su song ste zhes bya ba nas brtsams nas sems can de dag de nas thar te theg pa gsum po dag gis rim gyis sdug bsngal mthar 'byin pa mthong ngo zhes bya ba'i bar dang /_phyogs

[\[206b.1\]]bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi dud 'gro'i skye gnas kyi sems can rnams kyi don du bdag yongs su gtong ba la sogs pas dud 'gro'i skye gnas zhi ba'i phrin las dang /_de bzhin du yi dgas kyi yul gyi sdug bsngal rgyun gcod [#]pas gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi sdug bsngal zhi ba'i phrin las

[\[206b.4\]]'dis ni mi'i 'gro ba zhi ba'i phrin las dang /_gal te byang chub sems dpas kyang sems can rnams rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid thob par byed pa de lta yin na sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' la khyad par med par thal bas brtsad pa dang /_gnyi ga'ang ched du bya ba gcig
[\[206b.5\]]pa yin gyi/_mngon du byed pa dang mi byed pas ni ma yin no zhes de ltar khyad par [#]khas blangs pa'i lan btab pas gsungs pa yin no/_/bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi la 'god pa ni/_phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sems can rnams sbyin pa dang /_snyan par smra ba

[\[207a.1\]]sprul pa dper brjod pa dang bcas pas chos thams cad ma bcings ma grol ba nyid dang /_mi gnas pa'i sbyor ba dang 'phags pa'i gang zag thams cad la mnyes [#]par byas pa ma yin pa nas/_chos kyi dbyings dang de bzhin nyid dang yang dag pa'i mtha' las kyang

[\[207a.4\]]pa dang /_gal te 'bras bu rnam par gzhag pa kun rdzob yin gyi/_don dam pa ma yin na byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad rgyun du zhugs pa la sogs pa'i dngos por thal ba dang /_de rnams kyi bden pa gnyis rab tu ma shes pa'i lan nas brtsams te/_'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi
[\[207a.5\]]khams dag char [#]rnam par bcad pas 'bras bu rnam par 'jog pa yin no zhes bya ba'i bar gyis kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba rnam par gzhag pa dang /_chos kyi dbyings char mi gcod pa yin na kun tu sbyor ba gsum spangs pas 'bras bu dang po yin pa dang /_'dod pa'i [# ]
[\[207a.6\]]'dod chags dang gnod sems bsrabs pa nyid lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu yin pa dang /_'og ma'i cha dang mthun pa'i kun tu sbyor ba lnga spangs pa phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu yin pa dang /_gong ma'i cha dang mthun pa'i kun tu sbyor ba lnga spangs pa dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu yin par
[\[207a.7\]]ji ltar 'gyur zhes bya ba nas rgya cher byang chub ces bya ba'i bar gyi 'bras bu char dbye ba med par 'gyur bas dris pa dang /_dus gang gi tshe skad cig ma gcig gis chos thams cad rtogs pa zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa dper brjod pa dang bcas pa nas chos kyi mtshan nyid rtogs pa

[\[208a.1\]]pa yin no/_/brda las byung ba shes pa 'gog [#]pa ni/_de'i 'og tu gnas brtan rab 'byor bdag nyid dbang du byas pa'i dpes chos thams cad [#]rab tu 'jog pa'i phrin las kyis gang gsungs pa yin no/_/dmigs su med pa'i ye shes la [# ]
